24#define FR_PACKET_HEAD_0 0xEF
25#define FR_PACKET_HEAD_1 0xAA
26#define FR_PACKET_MIN_LEN 6
27#define FR_MAX_PACKET_LEN 128
28#define FR_REG_TIMEOUT_CNT 15000
29#define FR_MATCH_TIMEOUT_CNT 10000
30
31static uint8_t last_note = 0xFF;
32volatile uint8_t g_rx_lock = 0;
33
34static void fr_printf_recv(uint8_t *packet_buf, uint32_t packet_len)
35{
36#if FR_DEBUG_EN
37 uint32_t i;
38 if(packet_len < FR_PACKET_MIN_LEN || packet_buf[0] != FR_PACKET_HEAD_0 || packet_buf[1] != FR_PACKET_HEAD_1)
39 {
40 return;
41 }
42 printf("fr valid packet:");
43 for(i=0; i<packet_len; i++)
44 {
45 printf("%02X ", packet_buf[i]);
46 }
47 printf("\r\n");
48#else
49 (void)packet_buf;
50 (void)packet_len;
51#endif
52}

54// 【修复】增加缓冲区强制清空，防止数据溢出卡死
55static uint32_t fr_parse_packet(uint8_t *out_buf, uint32_t max_len)
56{
57 uint32_t i = 0;
58 uint32_t data_len = 0;
59 uint32_t total_len = 0;
60 g_rx_lock = 1;
61
62 // 溢出强制清空
63 if(g_usart6_rx_cnt >= sizeof(g_usart6_rx_buf))
64 {
65 g_usart6_rx_cnt = 0;
66 g_usart6_rx_end = 0;
67 memset((void*)g_usart6_rx_buf, 0, sizeof(g_usart6_rx_buf));
68 g_rx_lock = 0;
69 return 0;
70 }
71
72 for(i=0; i < g_usart6_rx_cnt - 1; i++)
73 {
74 if(g_usart6_rx_buf[i] == FR_PACKET_HEAD_0 && g_usart6_rx_buf[i+1] == FR_PACKET_HEAD_1)
75 {
76 break;
77 }
78 }
79 if(i >= g_usart6_rx_cnt - 1)
80 {
81 g_usart6_rx_cnt = 0;
82 g_usart6_rx_end = 0;
83 memset((void*)g_usart6_rx_buf, 0, sizeof(g_usart6_rx_buf));
84 g_rx_lock = 0;
85 return 0;
86 }
87 if(g_usart6_rx_cnt < i + FR_PACKET_MIN_LEN)
88 {
89 g_rx_lock = 0;
90 return 0;
91 }
92 data_len = (g_usart6_rx_buf[i+3] << 8) | g_usart6_rx_buf[i+4];
93 total_len = 6 + data_len;
94 if(total_len > FR_MAX_PACKET_LEN || total_len < FR_PACKET_MIN_LEN)
95 {
96 g_usart6_rx_cnt = 0;
97 g_usart6_rx_end = 0;
98 memset((void*)g_usart6_rx_buf, 0, sizeof(g_usart6_rx_buf));
99 g_rx_lock = 0;
100 return 0;
101 }
102 if(g_usart6_rx_cnt < i + total_len)
103 {
104 g_rx_lock = 0;
105 return 0;
106 }
107 if(total_len > max_len) total_len = max_len;
108 memcpy(out_buf, (uint8_t*)&g_usart6_rx_buf[i], total_len);
109 memmove((uint8_t*)&g_usart6_rx_buf[0], (uint8_t*)&g_usart6_rx_buf[i+total_len], g_usart6_rx_cnt - i - total_len);
110 g_usart6_rx_cnt -= (i + total_len);
111 g_usart6_rx_end = 0;
112 g_rx_lock = 0;
113 return total_len;
114}
115
116static uint8_t bcc_check(uint8_t *buf, uint32_t len)
117{
118 uint8_t check_sum = 0;
119 uint32_t i;
120 for(i=0; i<len; i++)
121 check_sum ^= buf[i];
122 return check_sum;
123}

125static void tim3_init(void)
126{
127 RCC_APB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_APB1Periph_TIM3, ENABLE);
128 TIM_TimeBaseStructure.TIM_Period = 10000/100-1;
129 TIM_TimeBaseStructure.TIM_Prescaler = 8400-1;
130 TIM_TimeBaseStructure.TIM_ClockDivision = 0;
131 TIM_TimeBaseStructure.TIM_CounterMode = TIM_CounterMode_Up;
132 TIM_TimeBaseInit(TIM3, &TIM_TimeBaseStructure);
133 TIM_ITConfig(TIM3,TIM_IT_Update,ENABLE);
134 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannel = TIM3_IRQn;
135 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelPreemptionPriority = 1;
136 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelSubPriority = 1;
137 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelCmd=ENABLE;
138 NVIC_Init(&NVIC_InitStructure);
139 TIM_Cmd(TIM3, DISABLE);
140}

142static void fr_reply_info(uint8_t reply)
143{
144#if FR_DEBUG_EN
145 if(reply==0)printf("[模块反馈] 操作成功\r\n");
146 if(reply==1)printf("[模块反馈] 模组拒绝该命令\r\n");
147 if(reply==2)printf("[模块反馈] 录入/匹配已终止\r\n");
148 if(reply==3)printf("[模块反馈] 发送消息错误\r\n");
149 if(reply==4)printf("[模块反馈] 相机打开失败\r\n");
150 if(reply==5)printf("[模块反馈] 未知错误\r\n");
151 if(reply==6)printf("[模块反馈] 无效的参数\r\n");
152 if(reply==7)printf("[模块反馈] 内存不足\r\n");
153 if(reply==8)printf("[模块反馈] 没有已录入的用户\r\n");
154 if(reply==9)printf("[模块反馈] 录入超过最大用户数量\r\n");
155 if(reply==10)printf("[模块反馈] 人脸已录入\r\n");
156 if(reply==12)printf("[模块反馈] 活体检测失败\r\n");
157 if(reply==13)printf("[模块反馈] 录入或解锁超时\r\n");
158 if(reply==14)printf("[模块反馈] 加密芯片授权失败\r\n");
159#else
160 (void)reply;
161#endif
162}

164static void fr_note_info(uint8_t note)
165{
166 if(note == last_note) return;
167 last_note = note;
168#if FR_DEBUG_EN
169 if(note==0)printf("[录入提示] 人脸正常，正在采集...\r\n");
170 if(note==1)printf("[录入提示] 未检测到人脸，请正对摄像头\r\n");
171 if(note==2)printf("[录入提示] 人脸太靠上，请下移\r\n");
172 if(note==3)printf("[录入提示] 人脸太靠下，请上移\r\n");
173 if(note==4)printf("[录入提示] 人脸太靠左，请右移\r\n");
174 if(note==5)printf("[录入提示] 人脸太靠右，请左移\r\n");
175 if(note==6)printf("[录入提示] 人脸太远，请靠近（0.4-1米）\r\n");
176 if(note==7)printf("[录入提示] 人脸太近，请后退\r\n");
177 if(note==8)printf("[录入提示] 眉毛被遮挡，请露出眉毛\r\n");
178 if(note==9)printf("[录入提示] 眼睛被遮挡，请露出眼睛\r\n");
179 if(note==10)printf("[录入提示] 脸部被遮挡，请露出完整脸部\r\n");
180 if(note==11)printf("[录入提示] 请正对摄像头，不要侧脸\r\n");
181#else
182 (void)note;
183#endif
184}
185
186void fr_send(uint8_t *buf, uint32_t len)
187{
188 uint8_t *p = buf;
189 g_rx_lock = 1;
190 g_usart6_rx_end = 0;
191 g_usart6_rx_cnt = 0;
192 last_note = 0xFF;
193 memset((void *)g_usart6_rx_buf, 0, sizeof(g_usart6_rx_buf));
194 g_rx_lock = 0;
195 while(len--)
196 {
197 USART_SendData(USART6, *p++);
198 while(!USART_GetFlagStatus(USART6, USART_FLAG_TXE));
199 USART_ClearFlag(USART6, USART_FLAG_TXE);
200 }
201}

203// 【修复】增加强制退出机制，杜绝死循环卡死
204int32_t fr_reg_user(const char *name, uint8_t is_admin)
205{
206 uint8_t buf_tx[64] = {0};
207 uint8_t packet_buf[FR_MAX_PACKET_LEN] = {0};
208 uint32_t packet_len = 0;
209 uint32_t timeout = 0;
210 uint32_t retry_cnt = 0;
211
212 printf("\r\n==================== 人脸录入开始 ====================\r\n");
213 printf("请将人脸正对摄像头，保持0.4-1米距离，超时时间15秒\r\n");
214
215 buf_tx[0] = FR_PACKET_HEAD_0;
216 buf_tx[1] = FR_PACKET_HEAD_1;
217 buf_tx[2] = 0x1D;
218 buf_tx[3] = 0x00;
219 buf_tx[4] = 0x23;
220 buf_tx[5] = is_admin;
221 if(name != NULL)
222 memcpy(&buf_tx[6], name, strlen(name));
223 buf_tx[38] = 0x00;
224 buf_tx[39] = 0x0A;
225 buf_tx[40] = bcc_check(&buf_tx[2], 38);
226 fr_send(buf_tx, 41);
227
228 while(1)
229 {
230 if(retry_cnt >= FR_REG_TIMEOUT_CNT)
231 {
232 printf("[人脸录入] 15秒超时，录入终止！\r\n");
233 beep_on();delay_ms(200);beep_off();delay_ms(100);beep_on();delay_ms(200);beep_off();
234 return -1;
235 }
236 retry_cnt++;
237 delay_ms(1);
238
239 timeout = 3000;
240 while(!g_usart6_rx_end && (--timeout)) delay_ms(1);
241 if(timeout == 0) continue;
242
243 packet_len = fr_parse_packet(packet_buf, sizeof(packet_buf));
244 if(packet_len == 0) continue;
245 fr_printf_recv(packet_buf, packet_len);
246
247 if(packet_buf[2] == 0)
248 {
249 uint8_t reply = packet_buf[6];
250 fr_reply_info(reply);
251 if(reply == 0)
252 {
253 printf("[人脸录入] 注册用户成功！\r\n");
254 beep_on();delay_ms(500);beep_off();
255 }
256 else
257 {
258 printf("[人脸录入] 注册用户失败！\r\n");
259 beep_on();delay_ms(200);beep_off();delay_ms(100);beep_on();delay_ms(200);beep_off();
260 }
261 return reply;
262 }
263 else if(packet_buf[2] == 1)
264 {
265 fr_note_info(packet_buf[6]);
266 continue;
267 }
268 }
269 return -1;
270}
271
272int32_t fr_match(uint8_t *buf)
273{
274 uint8_t buf_tx[8] = {0};
275 uint8_t packet_buf[FR_MAX_PACKET_LEN] = {0};
276 uint32_t packet_len = 0;
277 uint32_t timeout = 0;
278 uint32_t retry_cnt = 0;
279
280 printf("\r\n==================== 人脸匹配开始 ====================\r\n");
281 printf("请将人脸正对摄像头\r\n");
282
283 buf_tx[0] = FR_PACKET_HEAD_0;
284 buf_tx[1] = FR_PACKET_HEAD_1;
285 buf_tx[2] = 0x12;
286 buf_tx[3] = 0x00;
287 buf_tx[4] = 0x02;
288 buf_tx[5] = 0x01;
289 buf_tx[6] = 0x0A;
290 buf_tx[7] = bcc_check(&buf_tx[2], 5);
291 fr_send(buf_tx, 8);
292
293 while(1)
294 {
295 if(retry_cnt >= FR_MATCH_TIMEOUT_CNT)
296 {
297 return -1;
298 }
299 retry_cnt++;
300 delay_ms(1);
301
302 timeout = 3000;
303 while(!g_usart6_rx_end && (--timeout)) delay_ms(1);
304 if(timeout == 0) continue;
305
306 packet_len = fr_parse_packet(packet_buf, sizeof(packet_buf));
307 if(packet_len == 0) continue;
308 fr_printf_recv(packet_buf, packet_len);
309
310 if(packet_buf[2] == 1)
311 {
312 uint8_t note = packet_buf[6];
313 if(note == 1) printf("[匹配提示] 未检测到人脸\r\n");
314 else fr_note_info(note);
315 continue;
316 }
317 else if(packet_buf[2] == 0)
318 {
319 uint8_t reply = packet_buf[6];
320 fr_reply_info(reply);
321 if(reply != 0)
322 {
323 printf("[人脸匹配] 匹配失败！\r\n");
324 return reply;
325 }
326 if(buf != NULL) memcpy(buf, &packet_buf[7], 36);
327 printf("[人脸匹配] 匹配成功！\r\n");
328 return 0;
329 }
330 }
331 return -1;
332}
333
334int32_t fr_del_user_all(void)
335{
336 uint8_t buf_tx[8] = {0};
337 uint8_t packet_buf[FR_MAX_PACKET_LEN] = {0};
338 uint32_t packet_len = 0;
339 uint32_t timeout = 3000;
340
341 buf_tx[0] = FR_PACKET_HEAD_0;
342 buf_tx[1] = FR_PACKET_HEAD_1;
343 buf_tx[2] = 0x21;
344 buf_tx[3] = 0x00;
345 buf_tx[4] = 0x00;
346 buf_tx[5] = 0x21;
347 fr_send(buf_tx, 6);
348
349 while(!g_usart6_rx_end && (--timeout)) delay_ms(1);
350 if(timeout == 0) return -1;
351 packet_len = fr_parse_packet(packet_buf, sizeof(packet_buf));
352 if(packet_len == 0) return -1;
353 fr_printf_recv(packet_buf, packet_len);
354 if(packet_buf[5] == 0x21)
355 {
356 if(packet_buf[2]==0) fr_reply_info(packet_buf[6]);
357 return packet_buf[6];
358 }
359 return -1;
360}
361
362int32_t fr_get_user_total(void)
363{
364 int32_t user_total = 0;
365 uint8_t packet_buf[FR_MAX_PACKET_LEN] = {0};
366 uint32_t packet_len = 0;
367 uint32_t timeout = 4000;
368 uint8_t buf_tx[6] = {0};
369
370 buf_tx[0] = FR_PACKET_HEAD_0;
371 buf_tx[1] = FR_PACKET_HEAD_1;
372 buf_tx[2] = 0x24;
373 buf_tx[3] = 0x00;
374 buf_tx[4] = 0x00;
375 buf_tx[5] = 0x24;
376 fr_send(buf_tx, 6);
377
378 while(!g_usart6_rx_end && (--timeout)) delay_ms(1);
379 if(timeout == 0) return -1;
380 packet_len = fr_parse_packet(packet_buf, sizeof(packet_buf));
381 if(packet_len == 0) return -1;
382 fr_printf_recv(packet_buf, packet_len);
383 if((packet_buf[2]==0) && (packet_buf[5]==0x24) && (packet_buf[6]==0))
384 {
385 user_total = packet_buf[7];
386 return user_total;
387 }
388 return 0;
389}
390
391int32_t fr_reset(void)
392{
393 uint8_t buf_tx[6] = {0};
394 uint8_t packet_buf[FR_MAX_PACKET_LEN] = {0};
395 uint32_t packet_len = 0;
396 uint32_t timeout = 4000;
397
398 buf_tx[0] = FR_PACKET_HEAD_0;
399 buf_tx[1] = FR_PACKET_HEAD_1;
400 buf_tx[2] = 0x10;
401 buf_tx[3] = 0x00;
402 buf_tx[4] = 0x00;
403 buf_tx[5] = 0x10;
404 fr_send(buf_tx, 6);
405
406 while(!g_usart6_rx_end && (--timeout)) delay_ms(1);
407 if(timeout == 0) return -1;
408 packet_len = fr_parse_packet(packet_buf, sizeof(packet_buf));
409 if(packet_len == 0) return -1;
410 fr_printf_recv(packet_buf, packet_len);
411 if((packet_buf[2]==0) && (packet_buf[5]==0x10) && (packet_buf[6]==0x00))
412 {
413 return 0;
414 }
415 return -1;
416}

418int32_t fr_init(uint32_t baud)
419{
420 tim3_init();
421 usart6_init(baud);
422 delay_ms(500);
423 return fr_reset();
424}

426void TIM3_IRQHandler(void)
427{
428 if(TIM_GetITStatus(TIM3, TIM_IT_Update) == SET)
429 {
430 if(g_rx_lock == 0)
431 {
432 g_usart6_rx_end = 1;
433 }
434 TIM_Cmd(TIM3, DISABLE);
435 TIM_ClearITPendingBit(TIM3, TIM_IT_Update);
436 }
437}

443// 新增：人脸按键处理函数（迁移自main.c的while(1)）
444int32_t fr_process_face_key(uint8_t *face_key_sta, uint8_t *buf)
445{
446 if(face_key_sta == NULL || buf == NULL)
447 {
448 printf("[人脸识别模块] 参数错误！\r\n");
449 return -1;
450 }
451
452 /* 添加人脸 */
453 if((*face_key_sta) & 0x01)
454 {
455 __set_PRIMASK(1); // 关中断，保护标志位
456 (*face_key_sta) &= ~0x01;
457 __set_PRIMASK(0); // 开中断
458
459 printf("\r\n\r\n=====================================\r\n\r\n");
460 printf("[人脸识别模块] 执行人脸添加操作,请将脸部对准摄像头区，距离 0.4m ~ 1m \r\n");
461
462 if(0 == fr_reg_user(NULL,0))
463 {
464 printf("[人脸识别模块] 注册用户成功!\r\n");
465 beep_on();delay_ms(100);beep_off();
466 }
467 else
468 {
469 printf("[人脸识别模块] 注册用户失败!\r\n");
470 }
471 (*face_key_sta) = 0;
472 }
473
474 /* 刷人脸 */
475 if((*face_key_sta) & 0x02)
476 {
477 __set_PRIMASK(1);
478 (*face_key_sta) &= ~0x02;
479 __set_PRIMASK(0);
480
481 printf("\r\n\r\n=====================================\r\n\r\n");
482 printf("执行人脸匹配操作,请将脸部对准摄像头区，距离 0.4m ~ 1m \r\n");
483
484 if(0 == fr_match(buf))
485 {
486 printf("[人脸识别模块] 人脸匹配成功!\r\n");
487 SmartLock_ShowScanning();
488 SmartLock_ShowWelcome();
489 Lock_Set_Relay(1);
490 beep_on();
491 delay_s(1);
492 beep_off();
493 delay_s(2);
494 Lock_Set_Relay(0);
495 SmartLock_ShowBootScreen();
496 }
497 else
498 {
499 printf("[人脸识别模块] 人脸匹配失败!\r\n");
500 }
501 (*face_key_sta) = 0;
502 }
503
504 /* 删除所有用户 */
505 if((*face_key_sta) & 0x08)
506 {
507 __set_PRIMASK(1);
508 (*face_key_sta) &= ~0x08;
509 __set_PRIMASK(0);
510
511 printf("\r\n\r\n=====================================\r\n\r\n");
512 if(0 == fr_del_user_all())
513 {
514 printf("[人脸识别模块] 删除所有用户成功!\r\n");
515 beep_on();delay_ms(100);beep_off();
516 }
517 else
518 {
519 printf("[人脸识别模块] 删除所有用户失败!\r\n");
520 }
521 (*face_key_sta) = 0;
522 }
523
524 return 0;
525}

5void beep_init(void)
6{
7 GPIO_InitTypeDef GPIO_InitStructure;
8
9 //打开端口F的硬件时钟，就是对端口F供电
10 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOF,ENABLE);
11
12
13 //配置GPIOF的第9 10根
14 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin = GPIO_Pin_8;
15 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_OUT;
16 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Speed = GPIO_High_Speed;
17 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_OType = GPIO_OType_PP;
18 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_NOPULL;
19
20 //初始化
21 GPIO_Init(GPIOF,&GPIO_InitStructure);
22
23 PFout(8)=0;
24}

27{
28 PFout(8)=1;
29
30}

33{
34 PFout(8)=0;
35
36}

10// 蓝牙全局变量
11volatile u8 bt_rx_buffer[BT_RX_BUF_SIZE] = {0};
12volatile u8 bt_rx_count = 0;
13volatile u8 bt_rx_flag = 0;
14volatile u32 bt_heartbeat_timer = BT_HEARTBEAT_MAX;
15
16// 蓝牙初始化（精准波特率+中断优先级优化）
17void BT_Init(u32 baudrate)
18{
19 GPIO_InitTypeDef GPIO_InitStruct;
20 USART_InitTypeDef USART_InitStruct;
21 NVIC_InitTypeDef NVIC_InitStructure;
22
23 // 时钟使能
24 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOA, ENABLE);
25 RCC_APB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_APB1Periph_USART2, ENABLE);
26
27 // 引脚复用配置
28 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Pin = BT_TX_PIN | BT_RX_PIN;
29 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_AF;
30 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Speed = GPIO_Speed_50MHz;
31 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_OType = GPIO_OType_PP;
32 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_UP;
33 GPIO_Init(BT_PORT, &GPIO_InitStruct);
34
35 GPIO_PinAFConfig(BT_PORT, GPIO_PinSource2, GPIO_AF_USART2);
36 GPIO_PinAFConfig(BT_PORT, GPIO_PinSource3, GPIO_AF_USART2);
37
38 // 串口参数 8N1 无流控
39 USART_InitStruct.USART_BaudRate = baudrate;
40 USART_InitStruct.USART_WordLength = USART_WordLength_8b;
41 USART_InitStruct.USART_StopBits = USART_StopBits_1;
42 USART_InitStruct.USART_Parity = USART_Parity_No;
43 USART_InitStruct.USART_HardwareFlowControl = USART_HardwareFlowControl_None;
44 USART_InitStruct.USART_Mode = USART_Mode_Rx | USART_Mode_Tx;
45 USART_Init(USART2, &USART_InitStruct);
46
47 // 中断配置
48 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannel = USART2_IRQn;
49 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelPreemptionPriority = 2;
50 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelSubPriority = 1;
51 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelCmd = ENABLE;
52 NVIC_Init(&NVIC_InitStructure);
53
54 // 开启接收中断+串口使能
55 USART_ITConfig(USART2, USART_IT_RXNE, ENABLE);
56 USART_Cmd(USART2, ENABLE);
57
58 // 初始化清空缓冲区
59 bt_rx_count = 0;
60 bt_rx_flag = 0;
61 memset((void*)bt_rx_buffer, 0, BT_RX_BUF_SIZE);
62}
63
64// 单字节发送（超时防卡死）
65void BT_SendChar(u8 ch)
66{
67 u32 timeout = 0xFFFF;
68 USART_SendData(USART2, ch);
69 while(USART_GetFlagStatus(USART2, USART_FLAG_TXE) == RESET)
70 {
71 if(timeout-- == 0) break;
72 }
73}
74
75// 字符串发送（仅蓝牙专用，不与printf冲突）
76void BT_SendString(char *str)
77{
78 while(*str != '\0')
79 {
80 BT_SendChar((u8)*str);
81 str++;
82 }
83}
84
85// USART2蓝牙中断服务函数（过滤乱码+精准接收）
86void USART2_IRQHandler(void)
87{
88 u8 data;
89 if(USART_GetITStatus(USART2, USART_IT_RXNE) != RESET)
90 {
91 data = USART_ReceiveData(USART2);
92 bt_heartbeat_timer = 0; // 刷新心跳
93
94 // 过滤非可见字符+回车换行，杜绝乱码
95 if(data < 0x20 && data != ':' && data != '\r' && data != '\n')
96 {
97 USART_ClearITPendingBit(USART2, USART_IT_RXNE);
98 return;
99 }
100
101 if(bt_rx_count < BT_RX_BUF_SIZE - 1)
102 {
103 if(data == ':') // 指令结束符
104 {
105 bt_rx_buffer[bt_rx_count] = '\0';
106 bt_rx_flag = 1;
107 }
108 else if(data != '\r' && data != '\n') // 忽略换行
109 {
110 bt_rx_buffer[bt_rx_count++] = data;
111 }
112 }
113 else // 缓冲区溢出重置
114 {
115 bt_rx_count = 0;
116 bt_rx_flag = 0;
117 memset((void*)bt_rx_buffer, 0, BT_RX_BUF_SIZE);
118 }
119 USART_ClearITPendingBit(USART2, USART_IT_RXNE);
120 }
121}
122
123// 蓝牙指令处理（纯蓝牙数据，无调试串扰）
124void BT_ProcessCommand(void)
125{
126 if(bt_rx_flag)
127 {
128 bt_rx_flag = 0;
129 if(strstr((const char*)bt_rx_buffer, "OPEN") != NULL)
130 {
131 SmartLock_ShowScanning();
132 delay_ms(1000);
133 SmartLock_ShowWelcome();
134 BT_SendString("Door Opened.\r\n");
135 Lock_Set_Relay(1);
136 delay_s(3);
137 Lock_Set_Relay(0);
138 SmartLock_ShowBootScreen();
139 }
140 else if(strstr((const char*)bt_rx_buffer, "CLOSE") != NULL)
141 {
142 SmartLock_ShowDenied();
143 BT_SendString("Door Closed.\r\n");
144 delay_s(2);
145 SmartLock_ShowBootScreen();
146 }
147 else
148 {
149 BT_SendString("Unknown Command.\r\n");
150 }
151 // 清空缓冲区
152 bt_rx_count = 0;
153 memset((void*)bt_rx_buffer, 0, BT_RX_BUF_SIZE);
154 }
155 bt_heartbeat_timer++; // 心跳计时
156}

1#include "delay.h"
2
3u32 my_us = 21; //在21MHZ下，计21个数用时1us
4u32 my_ms = 21000; //在21MHZ下，计21000个数用时1ms
5
6void Delay_Init(void)
7{
8 //Systick的频率:168MHZ/8 = 21MHZ
9 SysTick_CLKSourceConfig(SysTick_CLKSource_HCLK_Div8);
10
11}
12
13//int nus取值范围:1~798915
14void delay_us(int nus) //10us
15{
16 u32 temp = 0;
17
18 //210
19 //设置重装载寄存器的值
20 SysTick->LOAD = nus*my_us - 1;
21
22 //设置计数器值为0
23 SysTick->VAL = 0x00;
24
25 //启动定时器,重装载寄存器的值会装载到计数器当中
26 SysTick->CTRL |= (0x01<<0);
27
28 do
29 {
30 temp = SysTick->CTRL;
31 //判断16位是否为1，为1表示计数器计数到0，则完成一次计数定时
32 //(temp & 0x01)判断定时器是否关闭 (temp & (0x01<<16))判断计数器是否计数到0
33 }while((temp & 0x01) && !(temp & (0x01<<16)));
34
35 //关闭定时器
36 SysTick->CTRL &= ~(0x01<<0);
37
38}
39
40//int nms取值范围: 理论上受SysTick限制，此处增加分段延时以支持大数值
41void delay_ms(int nms)
42{
43 while(nms > 500)
44 {
45 delay_ms(500);
46 nms -= 500;
47 }
48 u32 temp = 0;
49
50 //设置重装载寄存器的值
51 SysTick->LOAD = nms*my_ms - 1;
52
53 //设置计数器值为0
54 SysTick->VAL = 0x00;
55
56 //启动定时器
57 SysTick->CTRL |= (0x01<<0);
58
59 do
60 {
61 temp = SysTick->CTRL;
62 }while((temp & 0x01) && !(temp & (0x01<<16)));
63
64 //关闭定时器
65 SysTick->CTRL &= ~(0x01<<0);
66}
67
68void delay_s(int ns)
69{
70 for(int i = 0; i<ns; i++)
71 {
72 delay_ms(500);
73 delay_ms(500);
74 }
75
76}
77
78
79
80
81//粗延时(就是延时不一定准确的意思)
82void delay(int n)
83{
84 int i, j;
85
86 for(i=0; i<n; i++)
87 for(j=0; j<15000; j++);
88}

11volatile u8 esp8266_rx_flag = 0;

13volatile u8 g_bemfa_connected = 0;

18// USART3: TX=PB10, RX=PB11
19void ESP8266_Init(u32 baudrate)
20{
21 GPIO_InitTypeDef GPIO_InitStruct;
22 USART_InitTypeDef USART_InitStruct;
23 NVIC_InitTypeDef NVIC_InitStructure;
24
25 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOB, ENABLE);
26 RCC_APB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_APB1Periph_USART3, ENABLE);
27
28 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Pin = GPIO_Pin_10 | GPIO_Pin_11;
29 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_AF;
30 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Speed = GPIO_Speed_50MHz;
31 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_OType = GPIO_OType_PP;
32 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_UP;
33 GPIO_Init(GPIOB, &GPIO_InitStruct);
34
35 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOB, GPIO_PinSource10, GPIO_AF_USART3);
36 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOB, GPIO_PinSource11, GPIO_AF_USART3);
37
38 USART_InitStruct.USART_BaudRate = baudrate;
39 USART_InitStruct.USART_WordLength = USART_WordLength_8b;
40 USART_InitStruct.USART_StopBits = USART_StopBits_1;
41 USART_InitStruct.USART_Parity = USART_Parity_No;
42 USART_InitStruct.USART_HardwareFlowControl = USART_HardwareFlowControl_None;
43 USART_InitStruct.USART_Mode = USART_Mode_Rx | USART_Mode_Tx;
44 USART_Init(USART3, &USART_InitStruct);
45
46 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannel = USART3_IRQn;
47 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelPreemptionPriority = 1;
48 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelSubPriority = 2;
49 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelCmd = ENABLE;
50 NVIC_Init(&NVIC_InitStructure);
51
52 USART_ITConfig(USART3, USART_IT_RXNE, ENABLE);
53 USART_ITConfig(USART3, USART_IT_IDLE, ENABLE);
54 USART_Cmd(USART3, ENABLE);
55}
56
57void ESP8266_SendChar(u8 ch)
58{
59 USART_SendData(USART3, ch);
60 while(USART_GetFlagStatus(USART3, USART_FLAG_TXE) == RESET);
61}

63void ESP8266_SendString(char *str)
64{
65 while(*str != '\0')
66 {
67 ESP8266_SendChar(*str);
68 str++;
69 }
70}

72void ESP8266_ClearBuf(void)
73{
74 memset((void*)esp8266_rx_buffer, 0, ESP8266_RX_BUF_SIZE);
75 esp8266_rx_count = 0;
76 esp8266_rx_flag = 0;
77}
78
79u8 ESP8266_SendCmd(char *cmd, char *ack, u16 waittime)
80{
81 ESP8266_ClearBuf();
82 ESP8266_SendString(cmd);
83
84 while(waittime--)
85 {
86 delay_ms(10);
87 if(esp8266_rx_flag)
88 {
89 if(strstr((const char*)esp8266_rx_buffer, ack) != NULL)
90 {
91 return 1;
92 }
93 esp8266_rx_flag = 0;
94 }
95 }
96 printf("CMD Timeout: %s\r\n", cmd);
97 return 0;
98}
99
100u8 ESP8266_ConnectWiFi(char *ssid, char *pwd)
101{
102 char cmd[100];
103
104 ESP8266_SendString("+++");
105 delay_ms(1000);
106
107 ESP8266_SendCmd("AT+RST\r\n", "ready", 300);
108 delay_ms(1000);
109
110 if(ESP8266_SendCmd("AT+CWMODE=1\r\n", "OK", 50) == 0) return 0;
111
112 sprintf(cmd, "AT+CWJAP=\"%s\",\"%s\"\r\n", ssid, pwd);
113 if(ESP8266_SendCmd(cmd, "WIFI GOT IP", 1500) == 0)
114 {
115 if(ESP8266_SendCmd(cmd, "OK", 500) == 0) return 0;
116 }
117
118 return 1;
119}
120
121// 巴法云重连函数
122u8 ESP8266_ReconnectBemfa(char *uid, char *topic)
123{
124 char cmd[100];
125 g_bemfa_connected = 0; // 先标记为未连接
126
127 // 1. 退出透传模式
128 ESP8266_SendString("+++");
129 delay_ms(1500); // 必须延时1.5秒以上确保退出透传
130
131 // 2. 断开旧连接
132 ESP8266_SendCmd("AT+CIPCLOSE\r\n", "OK", 100);
133 delay_ms(500);
134
135 // 3. 设置单连接模式
136 if(ESP8266_SendCmd("AT+CIPMUX=0\r\n", "OK", 50) == 0)
137 {
138 printf("CIPMUX set failed\r\n");
139 return 0;
140 }
141
142 // 4. 连接巴法云服务器（多方式重试）
143 if(ESP8266_SendCmd("AT+CIPSTART=\"TCP\",\"bemfa.com\",8344,7200\r\n", "OK", 1500) == 0)
144 {
145 if(ESP8266_SendCmd("AT+CIPSTART=\"TCP\",\"bemfa.com\",8344\r\n", "OK", 1500) == 0)
146 {
147 if(ESP8266_SendCmd("AT+CIPSTART=\"TCP\",\"114.116.241.121\",8344\r\n", "OK", 1500) == 0)
148 {
149 printf("Bemfa connect failed\r\n");
150 return 0;
151 }
152 }
153 }
154
155 // 5. 开启透传
156 if(ESP8266_SendCmd("AT+CIPMODE=1\r\n", "OK", 50) == 0)
157 {
158 printf("CIPMODE set failed\r\n");
159 return 0;
160 }
161
162 // 6. 开始透传
163 if(ESP8266_SendCmd("AT+CIPSEND\r\n", ">", 100) == 0)
164 {
165 printf("CIPSEND no > ack, continue...\r\n");
166 }
167
168 // 7. 发送订阅指令
169 sprintf(cmd, "cmd=1&uid=%s&topic=%s\r\n", uid, topic);
170 printf("Send Subscribe: %s", cmd);
171 ESP8266_SendString(cmd);
172 delay_ms(1000);
173
174 g_bemfa_connected = 1; // 标记为已连接
175 printf("Bemfa reconnect success\r\n");
176 return 1;
177}
178
179// 增强：带回复检测的Ping（检测Pong回复）
180u8 Bemfa_Ping_Check(void)
181{
182 ESP8266_ClearBuf();
183 ESP8266_SendString("ping\r\n");
184
185 // 等待2秒检测是否有Pong回复
186 for(u16 i=0; i<200; i++)
187 {
188 delay_ms(10);
189 if(esp8266_rx_flag)
190 {
191 if(strstr((const char*)esp8266_rx_buffer, "pong") != NULL)
192 {
193 esp8266_rx_flag = 0;
194 return 1; // 收到Pong，在线
195 }
196 esp8266_rx_flag = 0;
197 }
198 }
199 return 0; // 未收到Pong，离线
200}
201
202// 原Ping函数保留（兼容旧逻辑）
203void Bemfa_Ping(void)
204{
205 ESP8266_SendString("ping\r\n");
206}
207
208void USART3_IRQHandler(void)
209{
210 u8 data;
211 if(USART_GetITStatus(USART3, USART_IT_RXNE) != RESET)
212 {
213 data = USART_ReceiveData(USART3);
214 if(esp8266_rx_count < ESP8266_RX_BUF_SIZE - 1)
215 {
216 esp8266_rx_buffer[esp8266_rx_count++] = data;
217 }
218 USART_ClearITPendingBit(USART3, USART_IT_RXNE);
219 }
220
221 if(USART_GetITStatus(USART3, USART_IT_IDLE) != RESET)
222 {
223 data = USART3->SR;
224 data = USART3->DR;
225 esp8266_rx_buffer[esp8266_rx_count] = '\0';
226 esp8266_rx_flag = 1;
227 }
228}
229
230void ESP8266_ProcessBemfaCommand(void)
231{
232 if(esp8266_rx_flag)
233 {
234 esp8266_rx_flag = 0;
235 if(strstr((const char*)esp8266_rx_buffer, "msg=on") != NULL)
236 {
237 SmartLock_ShowScanning();
238 delay_ms(1000);
239 SmartLock_ShowWelcome();
240 Lock_Set_Relay(1);
241 delay_s(3);
242 Lock_Set_Relay(0);
243 SmartLock_ShowBootScreen();
244 }
245 else if(strstr((const char*)esp8266_rx_buffer, "msg=off") != NULL)
246 {
247 SmartLock_ShowDenied();
248 delay_s(2);
249 SmartLock_ShowBootScreen();
250 }
251 ESP8266_ClearBuf();
252 }
253}
254
255// 新增：心跳检测与重连处理函数（原main中的逻辑迁移至此）
256void ESP8266_Heartbeat_Reconnect_Process(char *ssid, char *pwd, char *uid, char *topic)
257{
258 // 原心跳逻辑：检测Ping回复，判断是否在线
259 if(++ping_cnt >= 3000)
260 {
261 ping_cnt = 0;
262 // 检测Ping回复，失败则标记为断线
263 if(Bemfa_Ping_Check() == 0)
264 {
265 g_bemfa_connected = 0;
266 printf("Bemfa Ping failed, mark offline\r\n");
267 }
268 }
269
270 // 断线重连逻辑（每隔1秒检测一次）
271 if(++reconnect_cnt >= BEMFA_RECONNECT_INTERVAL)
272 {
273 reconnect_cnt = 0;
274 if(g_bemfa_connected == 0)
275 {
276 HW_OLED_ShowString(6,0,"Bemfa ReConn...");
277 // 重连WiFi（可选：防止WiFi也断了）
278 if(ESP8266_ConnectWiFi(ssid, pwd) == 1)
279 {
280 // 重连巴法云
281 if(ESP8266_ReconnectBemfa(uid, topic) == 1)
282 {
283 HW_OLED_ShowString(6,0,"Bemfa OK ");
284 }
285 else
286 {
287 HW_OLED_ShowString(6,0,"Bemfa Fail ");
288 }
289 }
290 }
291 }
292}

11extern uint8_t face_key_sta;
12
13static uint8_t key4_lock = 0;
14
15void Exti_PA0_Init(void)
16{
17 GPIO_InitTypeDef GPIO_InitStructure;
18 NVIC_InitTypeDef NVIC_InitStructure;
19 EXTI_InitTypeDef EXTI_InitStructure;
20
21 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOA|RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOE,ENABLE);
22 RCC_APB2PeriphClockCmd(RCC_APB2Periph_SYSCFG,ENABLE);
23
24 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Mode=GPIO_Mode_IN;
25 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_PuPd=GPIO_PuPd_UP;
26 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin=GPIO_Pin_0;
27 GPIO_Init(GPIOA,&GPIO_InitStructure);
28 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin=GPIO_Pin_2|GPIO_Pin_3|GPIO_Pin_4;
29 GPIO_Init(GPIOE,&GPIO_InitStructure);
30
31 SYSCFG_EXTILineConfig(EXTI_PortSourceGPIOA,EXTI_PinSource0);
32 SYSCFG_EXTILineConfig(EXTI_PortSourceGPIOE,EXTI_PinSource2);
33 SYSCFG_EXTILineConfig(EXTI_PortSourceGPIOE,EXTI_PinSource3);
34 SYSCFG_EXTILineConfig(EXTI_PortSourceGPIOE,EXTI_PinSource4);
35
36 EXTI_InitStructure.EXTI_Line=EXTI_Line0|EXTI_Line2|EXTI_Line3|EXTI_Line4;
37 EXTI_InitStructure.EXTI_Mode=EXTI_Mode_Interrupt;
38 EXTI_InitStructure.EXTI_Trigger=EXTI_Trigger_Falling;
39 EXTI_InitStructure.EXTI_LineCmd=ENABLE;
40 EXTI_Init(&EXTI_InitStructure);
41
42 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannel=EXTI0_IRQn;
43 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelPreemptionPriority=2;
44 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelSubPriority=1;
45 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelCmd=ENABLE;
46 NVIC_Init(&NVIC_InitStructure);
47 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannel=EXTI2_IRQn;
48 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelPreemptionPriority=2;
49 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelSubPriority=2;
50 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelCmd=ENABLE;
51 NVIC_Init(&NVIC_InitStructure);
52 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannel=EXTI3_IRQn;
53 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelPreemptionPriority=2;
54 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelSubPriority=3;
55 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelCmd=ENABLE;
56 NVIC_Init(&NVIC_InitStructure);
57 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannel=EXTI4_IRQn;
58 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelPreemptionPriority=0;
59 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelSubPriority=3;
60 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelCmd=ENABLE;
61 NVIC_Init(&NVIC_InitStructure);
62}
63
64void EXTI0_IRQHandler(void)
65{
66 if(EXTI_GetITStatus(EXTI_Line0)==SET)
67 {
68 delay_ms(20);
69 if(GPIO_ReadInputDataBit(GPIOA, GPIO_Pin_0) == RESET)
70 {
71 if(g_enroll_step==0)
72 {
73 g_enroll_flag=1;
74 }
75 }
76 EXTI_ClearITPendingBit(EXTI_Line0);
77 }
78}
79
80// 移除PE2触发解锁模式的逻辑（解锁功能默认一直开启）
81void EXTI2_IRQHandler(void)
82{
83 if(EXTI_GetITStatus(EXTI_Line2)==SET)
84 {
85 delay_ms(20);
86 // 清空原有解锁触发逻辑，保留中断标志清除
87 EXTI_ClearITPendingBit(EXTI_Line2);
88 }
89}
90
91void EXTI3_IRQHandler(void)
92{
93 if(EXTI_GetITStatus(EXTI_Line3)==SET)
94 {
95 delay_ms(20);
96 if(GPIO_ReadInputDataBit(GPIOE, GPIO_Pin_3) == RESET)
97 {
98 if(g_enroll_step==0&&g_unlock_mode==0)
99 {
100 g_delete_all_flag=1;
101 }
102 }
103 EXTI_ClearITPendingBit(EXTI_Line3);
104 }
105}
106
107// 【修复】必须清除中断标志位！否则无限中断卡死
108void EXTI4_IRQHandler(void)
109{
110 if(EXTI_GetITStatus(EXTI_Line4)==SET)
111 {
112 delay_ms(20);
113 if(GPIO_ReadInputDataBit(GPIOE, GPIO_Pin_4) == RESET && (face_key_sta & 0x02) == 0)
114 {
115 printf("=== 【提示】执行人脸操识别作 ===\r\n");
116 face_key_sta = 0;
117 face_key_sta|=1<<1;
118 }
119 // 【核心修复】清除中断挂起标志
120 EXTI_ClearITPendingBit(EXTI_Line4);
121 }
122}

9/*******************************************
10I2C1_SCL --- PB8
11I2C1_SDA -- PB9
12ʹ��I2C1

14void I2C_GPIO_Config(void)
15{
16
17 GPIO_InitTypeDef GPIO_InitStructure;
18 I2C_InitTypeDef I2C_InitStructure;
19
20
21 //GPIOB��ʼ��
22 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOB, ENABLE);
23 //IICʱ��ʹ��
24 RCC_APB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_APB1Periph_I2C1, ENABLE);
25
26 /* Connect PXx to I2C_SCL*/
27 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOB, GPIO_PinSource8, GPIO_AF_I2C1);
28 /* Connect PXx to I2C_SDA*/
29 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOB, GPIO_PinSource9, GPIO_AF_I2C1);
30
31 /*!< Configure EEPROM_I2C pins: SCL */
32 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin = GPIO_Pin_8|GPIO_Pin_9;
33 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_AF; //����
34 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Speed = GPIO_Speed_50MHz;
35 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_OType = GPIO_OType_OD; //��© ����һ��д��©
36 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_UP;
37 GPIO_Init(GPIOB, &GPIO_InitStructure);
38
39
40
41 /* I2C ���� */
42 I2C_InitStructure.I2C_Mode = I2C_Mode_I2C; //I2Cģʽ
43 I2C_InitStructure.I2C_DutyCycle = I2C_DutyCycle_2; /* �ߵ�ƽ�����ȶ����͵�ƽ���ݱ仯 SCL ʱ���ߵ�ռ�ձ� */
44 I2C_InitStructure.I2C_OwnAddress1 = 0x11; //ָ��������I2C�豸��ַ �����ĵ�ַ�ǲ�����ӻ���ͬ����
45 I2C_InitStructure.I2C_Ack = I2C_Ack_Enable ; //Ackʹ��
46 I2C_InitStructure.I2C_AcknowledgedAddress = I2C_AcknowledgedAddress_7bit; /* I2C��Ѱַģʽ */
47 I2C_InitStructure.I2C_ClockSpeed = 400000; /* ͨ������ ���ֻ����400Kbps */
48
49 I2C_Init(I2C1, &I2C_InitStructure); /* I2C1 ��ʼ�� */
50
51
52 I2C_Cmd(I2C1, ENABLE); /* ʹ�� I2C1 */
53
54
55}
56
57//AT24C02д����
58uint32_t I2C_EE_PageWrite(u8 WriteAddr, u8* pBuffer, u8 NumByteToWrite)
59{
60 uint32_t timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
61 //�ȴ����߿���
62 while(I2C_GetFlagStatus(I2C1, I2C_FLAG_BUSY))
63 {
64 if((timeout--) == 0) return 0;
65 }
66
67
68 //�����ź�
69 I2C_GenerateSTART(I2C1, ENABLE);
70 //�ȴ���������(�ȴ���ʼλ����)
71 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
72 while(!I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_MODE_SELECT))
73 {
74 if((timeout--) == 0) return 0;
75 }
76
77 // /* Send EEPROM address for write */
78 // //�����豸��ַ����ִ��д����
79 I2C_Send7bitAddress(I2C1, 0xA0, I2C_Direction_Transmitter);
80 /* Test on EV6 and clear it */ //��ַ���ͽ���
81 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
82 while(!I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_TRANSMITTER_MODE_SELECTED))
83 {
84 if((timeout--) == 0) return 0;
85 }
86
87
88 /* Send the EEPROM's internal address to write to */
89 //����д���ݵ���ʼ��ַ
90 I2C_SendData(I2C1, WriteAddr);
91 /* Test on EV8 and clear it */ //�ж����ݼĴ���Ϊ��
92 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
93 while(! I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_BYTE_TRANSMITTED))
94 {
95 if((timeout--) == 0) return 0;
96 }
97
98 /* While there is data to be written */
99 while(NumByteToWrite--)
100 {
101 /* Send the current byte */
102 I2C_SendData(I2C1, *pBuffer);
103 /* Test on EV8 and clear it */
104 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
105 while (!I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_BYTE_TRANSMITTED))
106 {
107 if((timeout--) == 0) return 0;
108 }
109
110 /* Point to the next byte to be written */
111 pBuffer++;
112
113 }
114
115 /* Send STOP condition */
116 I2C_GenerateSTOP(I2C1, ENABLE);
117
118 return 1;
119}
120
121/**
122 * @brief ��EEPROM�����ȡһ������
123 * @param
124 * @arg pBuffer:��Ŵ�EEPROM��ȡ�����ݵĻ�����ָ��
125 * @arg WriteAddr:�������ݵ�EEPROM�ĵ�ַ
126 * @arg NumByteToWrite:Ҫ��EEPROM��ȡ���ֽ���
127 * @retval ��
128 */
129uint32_t I2C_EE_BufferRead(u8 ReadAddr, u8* pBuffer, u16 NumByteToRead)
130{
131 uint32_t timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
132
133 //�ȴ����߿���
134 while(I2C_GetFlagStatus(I2C1, I2C_FLAG_BUSY))
135 {
136 if((timeout--) == 0) return 0;
137 }
138
139 /* Send START condition */
140 I2C_GenerateSTART(I2C1, ENABLE);
141 /* Test on EV5 and clear it */
142 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
143 while(!I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_MODE_SELECT))
144 {
145 if((timeout--) == 0) return 0;
146 }
147
148
149 /* Send EEPROM address for write */
150 I2C_Send7bitAddress(I2C1, 0xA0, I2C_Direction_Transmitter);
151 /* Test on EV6 and clear it */
152 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
153 while(!I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_TRANSMITTER_MODE_SELECTED))
154 {
155 if((timeout--) == 0) return 0;
156 }
157 /* Clear EV6 by setting again the PE bit */
158
159 //�������Ͷ����ݵ���ʼ��ַ
160 I2C_SendData(I2C1, ReadAddr);
161 /* Test on EV8 and clear it */
162 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
163 while(!I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_BYTE_TRANSMITTED))
164 {
165 if((timeout--) == 0) return 0;
166 }
167
168 //�����ź�
169 /* Send STRAT condition a second time */
170 I2C_GenerateSTART(I2C1, ENABLE);
171 /* Test on EV5 and clear it */
172 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
173 while(!I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_MODE_SELECT))
174 {
175 if((timeout--) == 0) return 0;
176 }
177
178
179//�����豸��ַ��ִ�ж�����
180 I2C_Send7bitAddress(I2C1, 0xA1, I2C_Direction_Receiver);
181 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
182 while(!I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_RECEIVER_MODE_SELECTED))
183 {
184 if((timeout--) == 0) return 0;
185 }
186
187
188 /* While there is data to be read */
189 while(NumByteToRead--)
190 {
191
192 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
193 while(I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_BYTE_RECEIVED)==0)
194 {
195 if((timeout--) == 0) return 0;
196 }
197 /* Read a byte from the device */
198 *pBuffer = I2C_ReceiveData(I2C1);
199
200 /* Point to the next location where the byte read will be saved */
201 pBuffer++;
202
203 if(NumByteToRead > 0)
204 {
205 //������Ч�ź�
206 I2C_AcknowledgeConfig(I2C1, ENABLE);
207
208 }
209
210 }
211
212 /* Enable Acknowledgement to be ready for another reception */
213 //������ҵӦ��
214 I2C_AcknowledgeConfig(I2C1, DISABLE);
215
216 /* Send STOP Condition */
217 I2C_GenerateSTOP(I2C1, ENABLE);
218
219 return 0;
220}

272static const u8 oled_default_char[6] = {0x7E, 0x52, 0x52, 0x52, 0x7E, 0x00};
273
274static void OLED_WriteBytes(u8 control, const u8 *buffer, u16 length)
275{
276 uint32_t timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
277 while(I2C_GetFlagStatus(I2C1, I2C_FLAG_BUSY))
278 {
279 if((timeout--) == 0) return;
280 }
281
282 I2C_GenerateSTART(I2C1, ENABLE);
283 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
284 while(!I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_MODE_SELECT))
285 {
286 if((timeout--) == 0) return;
287 }
288
289 I2C_Send7bitAddress(I2C1, 0x78, I2C_Direction_Transmitter);
290 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
291 while(!I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_TRANSMITTER_MODE_SELECTED))
292 {
293 if((timeout--) == 0) return;
294 }
295
296 I2C_SendData(I2C1, control);
297 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
298 while(!I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_BYTE_TRANSMITTED))
299 {
300 if((timeout--) == 0) return;
301 }
302
303 while(length--)
304 {
305 I2C_SendData(I2C1, *buffer++);
306 timeout = I2C_TIMEOUT;
307 while(!I2C_CheckEvent(I2C1, I2C_EVENT_MASTER_BYTE_TRANSMITTED))
308 {
309 if((timeout--) == 0) return;
310 }
311 }
312 I2C_GenerateSTOP(I2C1, ENABLE);
313}
314
315static void OLED_WriteCommand(u8 cmd)
316{
317 OLED_WriteBytes(0x00, &cmd, 1);
318}
319
320static const u8 *OLED_GetCharData(char ch)
321{
322 u8 i;
323
324 for(i = 0; i < sizeof(oled_font_6x8) / sizeof(oled_font_6x8[0]); i++)
325 {
326 if(oled_font_6x8[i].ch == ch)
327 {
328 return oled_font_6x8[i].data;
329 }
330 }
331
332 return oled_default_char;
333}
334
335static void OLED_SetPosition(u8 page, u8 column)
336{
337 OLED_WriteCommand(0xB0 + page);
338 OLED_WriteCommand(0x00 + (column & 0x0F));
339 OLED_WriteCommand(0x10 + ((column >> 4) & 0x0F));
340}
341
342void HW_OLED_ShowString(u8 page, u8 column, const char *str)
343{
344 while(*str != '\0')
345 {
346 OLED_SetPosition(page, column);
347 OLED_WriteBytes(0x40, OLED_GetCharData(*str), 6);
348 column += 6;
349 str++;
350 }
351}
352
353void HW_OLED_Init(void)
354{
355 u8 init_cmds[] =
356 {
357 0xAE, 0x20, 0x10, 0xB0, 0xC8, 0x00, 0x10, 0x40,
358 0x81, 0x7F, 0xA1, 0xA6, 0xA8, 0x3F, 0xA4, 0xD3,
359 0x00, 0xD5, 0x80, 0xD9, 0xF1, 0xDA, 0x12, 0xDB,
360 0x20, 0x8D, 0x14, 0xAF
361 };
362 u8 i;
363 for(i = 0; i < sizeof(init_cmds) / sizeof(init_cmds[0]); i++)
364 {
365 OLED_WriteCommand(init_cmds[i]);
366 }
367}
368
369void HW_OLED_Clear(void)
370{
371 u8 page;
372 u8 clear_buffer[128];
373
374 memset(clear_buffer, 0, sizeof(clear_buffer));
375 for(page = 0; page < 8; page++)
376 {
377 OLED_SetPosition(page, 0);
378 OLED_WriteBytes(0x40, clear_buffer, sizeof(clear_buffer));
379 }
380}
381
382void OLED_ShowCenteredString(u8 page, const char *str)
383{
384 u8 len = strlen(str);
385 u8 column = (128 - len * 6) / 2;
386 HW_OLED_ShowString(page, column, str);
387}
388
389void SmartLock_ShowBootScreen(void)
390{
391 HW_OLED_Clear();
392
393 // "Smart Lock System" (17 chars -> 102 pixels)
394 HW_OLED_ShowString(2, (128 - 17 * 6) / 2, "Smart Lock System");
395
396 // Draw a separator line
397 OLED_SetPosition(4, 0);
398 for(u8 i=0; i<128; i++) OLED_WriteBytes(0x40, (u8[]){0x08}, 1);
399
400 // "Ready..." (8 chars -> 48 pixels)
401 HW_OLED_ShowString(6, (128 - 8 * 6) / 2, "Ready...");
402}
403
404void SmartLock_ShowScanning(void)
405{
406 HW_OLED_Clear();
407 OLED_ShowCenteredString(3, "Scanning...");
408}

411{
412 HW_OLED_Clear();
413 OLED_ShowCenteredString(3, "Unlock Success");
414}

417{
418 HW_OLED_Clear();

420}

430 HW_OLED_ShowString(0, 80, "BT:FAIL");
431 }

1#include "iwdg.h"
2
3void Iwdg_Init(void)
4{
5 //1、 取消寄存器写保护：
6 IWDG_WriteAccessCmd(IWDG_WriteAccess_Enable);
7 //2、设置独立看门狗的预分频系数，确定时钟:32kHZ/256 = 125HZ
8 IWDG_SetPrescaler(IWDG_Prescaler_256);
9 //3、设置看门狗重装载值，确定溢出时间:2s(2s必须喂狗)
10 IWDG_SetReload(250);
11 //4、使能看门狗
12 IWDG_Enable();
13 //5、应用程序喂狗: 计数从250开始倒数
14 IWDG_ReloadCounter();
15
16}

11extern uint8_t g_pwd_len;
12extern uint8_t g_saved_pwd[6];
13extern uint8_t g_setting_pwd_mode;
14extern uint8_t face_key_sta; // 人脸功能按键

22// 矩阵键盘初始化（彻底清除FSMC复用，强制普通GPIO模式）
23void KEY4X4_Init(void)
24{
25 GPIO_InitTypeDef GPIO_InitStructure;
26
27 // 1. 强制关闭FSMC时钟，彻底切断LCD对PE口的控制
28 RCC_AHB3PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB3Periph_FSMC, DISABLE);
29 // 2. 开启GPIOE时钟
30 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOE, ENABLE);
31
32 // 3. 【核心修正】强制清零所有引脚的复用寄存器，彻底解除复用
33 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOE, GPIO_PinSource7, GPIO_AF_RTC_50Hz); // 清零PE7复用
34 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOE, GPIO_PinSource8, GPIO_AF_RTC_50Hz); // 清零PE8复用
35 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOE, GPIO_PinSource9, GPIO_AF_RTC_50Hz); // 清零PE9复用
36 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOE, GPIO_PinSource10, GPIO_AF_RTC_50Hz); // 清零PE10复用
37 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOE, GPIO_PinSource11, GPIO_AF_RTC_50Hz); // 清零PE11复用
38 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOE, GPIO_PinSource12, GPIO_AF_RTC_50Hz); // 清零PE12复用
39 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOE, GPIO_PinSource13, GPIO_AF_RTC_50Hz); // 清零PE13复用
40 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOE, GPIO_PinSource14, GPIO_AF_RTC_50Hz); // 清零PE14复用
41
42 // 4. 先把所有引脚设为普通输入，彻底重置状态
43 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin = GPIO_Pin_7 | GPIO_Pin_8 | GPIO_Pin_9 | GPIO_Pin_10 |
44 GPIO_Pin_11 | GPIO_Pin_12 | GPIO_Pin_13 | GPIO_Pin_14;
45 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_IN;
46 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_NOPULL;
47 GPIO_Init(GPIOE, &GPIO_InitStructure);
48
49 // 5. 配置行线（PE7~PE10）：推挽输出
50 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin = ROW1_Pin | ROW2_Pin | ROW3_Pin | ROW4_Pin;
51 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_OUT;
52 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_OType = GPIO_OType_PP;
53 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Speed = GPIO_Speed_2MHz;
54 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_NOPULL;
55 GPIO_Init(GPIOE, &GPIO_InitStructure);
56
57 // 6. 配置列线（PE11~PE14）：上拉输入
58 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin = COL1_Pin | COL2_Pin | COL3_Pin | COL4_Pin;
59 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_IN;
60 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_UP;
61 GPIO_Init(GPIOE, &GPIO_InitStructure);
62
63 // 7. 初始所有行拉低，等待按键检测
64 GPIO_ResetBits(GPIOE, ROW1_Pin | ROW2_Pin | ROW3_Pin | ROW4_Pin);
65}
66
67// 按键扫描函数（修正行输出逻辑，确保逐行拉低可靠）
68uint8_t KEY4X4_Scan(void)
69{
70 static uint8_t key_up = 1; // 按键松开标志，1=松开，0=按下
71 uint8_t key_val = 100;
72
73 // ========== 第一步：先检测有没有按键按下（所有行先拉低） ==========
74 PEout(7) = 0; PEout(8) = 0; PEout(9) = 0; PEout(10) = 0;
75 delay_ms(2); // 等待电平稳定
76
77 // 如果没有按键按下，直接跳过扫描，减轻CPU占用
78 if(PEin(11) == 1 && PEin(12) == 1 && PEin(13) == 1 && PEin(14) == 1)
79 {
80 key_up = 1; // 标记按键松开
81 delay_ms(10);
82 return 100;
83 }
84
85 // ========== 第二步：只有按键按下且处于松开状态，才进入逐行扫描 ==========
86 if(key_up == 1)
87 {
88 delay_ms(20); // 【关键】先消抖20ms，过滤机械抖动
89
90 // 扫描第1行：拉低PE7，其他行拉高
91 PEout(7) = 0; PEout(8) = 1; PEout(9) = 1; PEout(10) = 1;
92 delay_ms(2);
93 if(PEin(11) == 0) { key_val = 1; goto KEY_END; } // 【关键】检测到按键直接跳转，避免后面行重复赋值
94 if(PEin(12) == 0) { key_val = 2; goto KEY_END; }
95 if(PEin(13) == 0) { key_val = 3; goto KEY_END; }
96 if(PEin(14) == 0) { key_val = 24; goto KEY_END; }
97
98 // 扫描第2行：拉低PE8，其他行拉高
99 PEout(7) = 1; PEout(8) = 0; PEout(9) = 1; PEout(10) = 1;
100 delay_ms(2);
101 if(PEin(11) == 0) { key_val = 4; goto KEY_END; }
102 if(PEin(12) == 0) { key_val = 5; goto KEY_END; }
103 if(PEin(13) == 0) { key_val = 6; goto KEY_END; }
104 if(PEin(14) == 0) { key_val = 25; goto KEY_END; }
105
106 // 扫描第3行：拉低PE9，其他行拉高
107 PEout(7) = 1; PEout(8) = 1; PEout(9) = 0; PEout(10) = 1;
108 delay_ms(2);
109 if(PEin(11) == 0) { key_val = 7; goto KEY_END; }
110 if(PEin(12) == 0) { key_val = 8; goto KEY_END; }
111 if(PEin(13) == 0) { key_val = 9; goto KEY_END; }
112 if(PEin(14) == 0) { key_val = 26; goto KEY_END; }
113
114 // 扫描第4行：拉低PE10，其他行拉高
115 PEout(7) = 1; PEout(8) = 1; PEout(9) = 1; PEout(10) = 0;
116 delay_ms(2);
117 if(PEin(11) == 0) { key_val = 0; goto KEY_END; }
118 if(PEin(12) == 0) { key_val = 27; goto KEY_END; }
119 if(PEin(13) == 0) { key_val = 28; goto KEY_END; } // 按键28
120 if(PEin(14) == 0) { key_val = 29; goto KEY_END; }
121 }
122
123KEY_END:
124 // ========== 第三步：按键处理，按下一次只输出一次 ==========
125 if(key_val != 100 && key_up == 1)
126 {
127 key_up = 0; // 【关键】立即标记按键按下，禁止重复触发
128
129 // 【关键】等待按键完全松开，才允许下一次触发
130 while(PEin(11) == 0 || PEin(12) == 0 || PEin(13) == 0 || PEin(14) == 0)
131 {
132 delay_ms(10);
133 }
134 key_up = 1; // 标记按键松开
135 delay_ms(20); // 松开后再消抖一次
136 }
137
138 return key_val;
139}
140
141void KEY4X4_Handle16Key(void)
142{
143 uint8_t key = KEY4X4_Scan();
144 if(key != 100)
145 {
146 printf("\r\n[按键触发] 原始键值：%d\r\n", key);
147 switch(key)
148 {
149 case 24:
150 printf("=== 【提示】进入修改密码模式 ===\r\n");
151 printf("请输入6位新密码，完成后按确定键(29)\r\n");
152 g_setting_pwd_mode = 1;
153 g_pwd_len = 0;
154 memset((void*)g_input_pwd, 0, sizeof(g_input_pwd));
155 Finger_Led(3);
156 break;
157 case 25:
158 printf("=== 【提示】已进入人脸录入模式 ===\r\n");
159 face_key_sta = 0;
160 face_key_sta|=1<<0;
161 break;
162 case 26:
163 printf("=== 【提示】执行删除所有人脸操作 ===\r\n");
164 face_key_sta = 0;
165 face_key_sta|=1<<3;
166 break;
167 // 新增：按键27处理 - 门卡录入模式
168 case 27:
169 printf("=== 【提示】进入门卡录入模式 ===\r\n");
170 printf("请将需要录入的门卡靠近读卡器...\r\n");
171 g_enroll_card_mode = 1; // 置位录入模式标志
172 Finger_Led(3); // 黄灯提示录入中
173 break;
174 // 新增：按键28处理 - 删除所有门卡
175 case 28:
176 printf("=== 【提示】执行删除所有门卡操作 ===\r\n");
177 RC522_DeleteAllCard(); // 调用删除所有门卡函数
178 Finger_Led(1); // 红灯提示操作
179 delay_ms(1000);
180 Finger_Led(4); // 恢复默认灯态
181 break;
182 case 29:
183 if (g_setting_pwd_mode == 1)
184 {
185 if (g_pwd_len == 6) {
186 memcpy((void*)g_saved_pwd, (void*)g_input_pwd, 6);
187 printf("=== 【提示】新密码设置成功！ ===\r\n");
188 Finger_Led(2);
189 delay_ms(1000);
190 } else {
191 printf("=== 【错误】密码必须是6位，设置失败！ ===\r\n");
192 Finger_Led(1);
193 delay_ms(1000);
194 }
195 g_pwd_len = 0;
196 memset((void*)g_input_pwd, 0, sizeof(g_input_pwd));
197 g_setting_pwd_mode = 0;
198 Finger_Led(4);
199 }
200 else
201 {
202 if (g_pwd_len > 0)
203 {
204 printf("=== 【提示】正在验证密码... ===\r\n");
205 if (g_pwd_len == 6 && memcmp((void*)g_input_pwd, (void*)g_saved_pwd, 6) == 0)
206 {
207 printf("=== 【提示】密码正确，开锁成功！ ===\r\n");
208 SmartLock_ShowWelcome();
209 Finger_Led(2);
210 Lock_Set_Relay(1);
211 delay_s(3);
212 Lock_Set_Relay(0);
213 SmartLock_ShowBootScreen();
214 }
215 else
216 {
217 printf("=== 【错误】密码错误，拒绝开锁！ ===\r\n");
218 SmartLock_ShowDenied();
219 Finger_Led(1);
220 delay_ms(2000);
221 SmartLock_ShowBootScreen();
222 }
223 g_pwd_len = 0;
224 memset((void*)g_input_pwd, 0, sizeof(g_input_pwd));
225 Finger_Led(4);
226 }
227 }
228 break;
229 default:
230 if (key >= 0 && key <= 9)
231 {
232 if (g_pwd_len < 6)
233 {
234 g_input_pwd[g_pwd_len] = key;
235 g_pwd_len++;
236 printf("输入: %d (当前进度: %d/6)\r\n", key, g_pwd_len);
237 }
238 else
239 {
240 printf("【提示】密码已达到6位，请按确定键(29)！\r\n");
241 }
242 }
243 break;
244 }
245 }
246}

7

18 //RCC_AHB1ENR |= RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOF;

20 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOE, ENABLE);
21

23 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_OUT;//输出模式
24 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_OType = GPIO_OType_PP; //输出推挽
25 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Speed = GPIO_Speed_25MHz;//速度
26 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_UP; //上拉

28
29
30
31 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Pin = GPIO_Pin_13|GPIO_Pin_14; //引脚
32 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_OUT;//输出模式
33 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_OType = GPIO_OType_PP; //输出推挽
34 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Speed = GPIO_Speed_25MHz;//速度
35 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_UP; //上拉
36 GPIO_Init(GPIOE, &GPIO_InitStruct);
37
38
39 GPIO_SetBits(GPIOF, GPIO_Pin_9);
40 GPIO_SetBits(GPIOF, GPIO_Pin_10);
41 GPIO_SetBits(GPIOE, GPIO_Pin_13);
42 GPIO_SetBits(GPIOE, GPIO_Pin_14);
43
44
45
46
47}

33// 定义_sys_exit()以避免使用半主机模式（半主机模式会导致程序依赖调试器运行）
34int _sys_exit(int x)

39// printf输出重定向到串口2：将printf的字符通过串口2发送，实现串口打印
40int fputc(int ch, FILE *f)
41{
42 uint32_t timeout = 0x1FFFF; // 发送超时阈值，防止死等
43 USART_SendData(USART2, ch); // 向串口2寄存器写入待发送字符
44 // 等待串口发送完成标志置位（TXE：发送数据寄存器空）
45 while(USART_GetFlagStatus(USART2, USART_FLAG_TXE) == RESET)
46 {
47 if(timeout-- == 0) break; // 超时退出，避免死循环
48 }
49 return ch;
50}

52// -------------------------- 全局变量定义 --------------------------
53volatile uint8_t g_buffer[8] = {0}; // 通用数据缓冲数组（8字节）
54volatile uint8_t g_rx_buffer[32] = {0}; // 串口/蓝牙/WiFi接收缓冲数组（32字节）
55volatile uint8_t g_cout = 0; // 数据接收/发送计数变量
56volatile uint8_t g_flag = 0; // 通用状态标志位
57volatile uint8_t g_enroll_flag = 0; // 指纹录入功能使能标志（0：未录入，1：录入中）
58volatile uint8_t g_enroll_step = 0; // 指纹录入步骤（0：未开始，1/2/3：录入阶段）
59volatile uint8_t g_unlock_flag = 0; // 解锁功能触发标志（0：未解锁，1：待解锁）
60volatile uint8_t g_unlock_mode = 1; // 解锁模式默认开启（修改：默认=1）
61volatile uint8_t g_delete_all_flag = 0; // 删除所有指纹标志（0：未删除，1：待删除）
62volatile uint8_t g_manual_finger_trigger = 0;// 手动触发指纹识别标志
63uint16_t user_id; // 指纹/用户ID（用于指纹模块用户管理）
64uint8_t g_input_pwd[6] = {0}; // 键盘输入密码缓冲（6位密码）
65uint8_t g_pwd_len = 0; // 输入密码的长度计数
66uint8_t g_saved_pwd[6] = {1,2,3,4,5,6}; // 系统保存的默认密码（123456）
67uint8_t g_setting_pwd_mode = 0; // 密码设置模式标志（0：未设置，1：设置中）
68uint8_t face_key_sta = 0; // 人脸功能按键
69uint8_t buf[64]={0}; // 人脸检测时所用数组
70// 自动寻卡标志：开机默认启动（置1）
71extern uint8_t Auto_Card_Flag;
72
73// -------------------------- 宏定义（应答码） --------------------------
74#define ACK_SUCCESS 0x00 // 操作成功应答码
75#define ACK_FAIL 0x01 // 操作失败应答码
76#define ACK_FULL 0x04 // 指纹库已满应答码
77#define ACK_NOUSER 0x05 // 无该用户（指纹/IC卡未注册）应答码
78#define ACK_USER_EXIST 0x07 // 用户已存在（指纹/IC卡重复注册）应答码
79#define ACK_TIMEOUT 0x08 // 操作超时应答码
80
81// -------------------------- 键盘防抖相关 --------------------------
82uint8_t key_debounce_cnt = 0; // 键盘防抖计数变量
83uint8_t key_sta = 1; // 键盘按键状态（1：未按下，0：按下）
84
85// -------------------------- WiFi/巴法云配置常量 --------------------------
86char bemfa_uid[] = "d3494acad6424a54bf8142d7a3e60cb9"; // 巴法云平台UID（设备唯一标识）
87char bemfa_topic[] = "VmOmMcv79006"; // 巴法云订阅主题（用于MQTT通信）
88char wifi_ssid[] = "BAT"; // WiFi名称（需修改为实际路由器SSID）
89char wifi_pwd[] = "3266433ok"; // WiFi密码（需修改为实际路由器密码）
90
91// -------------------------- 主函数（程序入口） --------------------------
92int main(void)
93{
94 // 1. 系统核心初始化
95 NVIC_PriorityGroupConfig(NVIC_PriorityGroup_2); // NVIC优先级分组：2位抢占优先级，2位响应优先级
96 Delay_Init(); // 延时函数初始化（SysTick定时器）
97 Led_Init(); // LED灯GPIO初始化（用于状态指示）
98 Usart1_Init(115200); // 串口1初始化（波特率115200，用于调试/RC522通信）
99 BT_Init(9600); // 蓝牙HC05初始化（波特率9600，蓝牙通信）
100 I2C_GPIO_Config(); // I2C总线GPIO初始化（用于OLED/EEPROM通信）
101 HW_OLED_Init(); // OLED显示屏初始化（显示系统状态）
102 Lock_Relay_Init(); // 门锁继电器GPIO初始化（控制锁的开关）
103 ESP8266_Init(115200); // ESP8266模块初始化（波特率115200，WiFi通信）
104 SmartLock_ShowBootScreen(); // 显示智能锁开机画面（OLED）
105
106 // 2. WiFi连接流程
107 HW_OLED_ShowString(5,0,"WiFi Conn..."); // OLED第5行显示"WiFi连接中..."
108 HW_OLED_ShowString(6,0,"Bemfa Conn..."); // OLED第6行显示"巴法云连接中..."
109 // 循环尝试连接WiFi，直到连接成功（返回非0）
110 while(ESP8266_ConnectWiFi(wifi_ssid, wifi_pwd)==0)
111 {
112 delay_ms(1000);
113 }
114 HW_OLED_ShowString(5,0,"WiFi OK "); // WiFi连接成功，更新OLED显示
115
116 // 3. 巴法云平台连接流程（MQTT协议）
117 // 循环尝试重连巴法云，直到连接成功
118 while(ESP8266_ReconnectBemfa(bemfa_uid, bemfa_topic)==0)
119 {
120 delay_ms(1000);
121 }
122 HW_OLED_ShowString(6,0,"Bemfa OK "); // 巴法云连接成功，更新OLED显示
123 delay_ms(2000); // 延时2秒，让用户看到连接成功状态
124 SmartLock_ShowBootScreen(); // 恢复显示开机画面
125
126 // 4. 外设初始化（人机交互/识别模块）
127 KEY4X4_Init(); // 4x4矩阵键盘初始化（密码输入）
128 zhi_init(); // 指纹识别模块初始化
129 Exti_PA0_Init(); // PA0外部中断初始化（用于指纹模块触发/按键中断）
130 Finger_Led(3); // 指纹模块LED灯初始化（3：蓝灯闪烁，提示等待指纹）
131 RC522_Init(); // RC522射频卡模块初始化（IC卡识别）
132 printf("自动寻卡模式已启动\r\n"); // 打印启动提示
133 printf("指纹解锁功能已默认开启\r\n"); // 新增：提示解锁功能开启
134
135 beep_init(); // 蜂鸣器初始化
136 printf("3D人脸识别模块测试程序\r\n");
137
138 while(fr_init(115200)!=0) //跟3D人脸识别模块进行握手
139 {
140 delay_ms(1000);
141 printf("3D人脸识别模块连接中 ...\r\n");
142 }
143 printf("3D人脸识别模块已连接上\r\n");
144
145 // 5. 启动完成提示
146 printf("系统启动完成\r\n"); // 串口打印启动完成信息（调试用）
147 BT_SendString("System Ready.\r\n"); // 蓝牙发送启动完成信息（手机端提示）
148
149 // 6. 主循环（系统核心逻辑）
150 while(1)
151 {
152 BT_ProcessCommand(); // 处理蓝牙接收到的命令（如蓝牙解锁/设置）
153 ESP8266_ProcessBemfaCommand(); // 处理巴法云平台下发的命令（如WiFi远程解锁）
154
155 // ESP8266心跳包发送+断网重连处理（核心：维持WiFi/巴法云连接）
156 ESP8266_Heartbeat_Reconnect_Process(wifi_ssid, wifi_pwd, bemfa_uid, bemfa_topic);
157
158 KEY4X4_Handle16Key(); // 处理矩阵键盘按键（密码输入/功能选择）
159 Finger_Enroll_Process(); // 指纹录入流程处理（录入新指纹）
160 Finger_Unlock_Trigger_Process(); // 空函数，解锁默认开启
161 Finger_Unlock_Mode_Process(); // 指纹解锁模式处理（一直开启，录入时关闭）
162 Finger_DeleteAll_Process(); // 删除所有指纹流程处理
163 RC522_Card_Process(); // RC522 IC卡识别流程（刷卡解锁）
164
165 fr_process_face_key(&face_key_sta, buf);
166
167 delay_ms(10); // 主循环延时10ms，降低CPU占用率
168 }
169}
1#include "oled.h"
2#include "oledfont.h"
3#include "delay.h"
4
5void OLED_IIC_Delay(void)
6{
7 u8 t=1;
8 while(t--);
9}
10
11void OLED_IIC_Start(void)
12{
13 OLED_SDA = 1;
14 OLED_SCL = 1;
15 OLED_IIC_Delay();
16 OLED_SDA = 0;
17 OLED_IIC_Delay();
18 OLED_SCL = 0;
19}
20
21void OLED_IIC_Stop(void)
22{
23 OLED_SDA = 0;
24 OLED_SCL = 1;
25 OLED_IIC_Delay();
26 OLED_SDA = 1;
27}
28
29void OLED_IIC_Wait_Ack(void)
30{
31 OLED_SCL = 1;
32 OLED_IIC_Delay();
33 OLED_SCL = 0;
34 OLED_IIC_Delay();
35}
36
37void OLED_IIC_Write_Byte(u8 data)
38{
39 u8 i;
40 for(i=0; i<8; i++)
41 {
42 if(data & 0x80) OLED_SDA = 1;
43 else OLED_SDA = 0;
44 OLED_SCL = 1;
45 OLED_IIC_Delay();
46 OLED_SCL = 0;
47 OLED_IIC_Delay();
48 data <<= 1;
49 }
50 OLED_IIC_Wait_Ack();
51}
52
53void OLED_Write_Cmd(u8 cmd)
54{
55 OLED_IIC_Start();
56 OLED_IIC_Write_Byte(0x78); // Slave address
57 OLED_IIC_Write_Byte(0x00); // Command mode
58 OLED_IIC_Write_Byte(cmd);
59 OLED_IIC_Stop();
60}
61
62void OLED_Write_Data(u8 data)
63{
64 OLED_IIC_Start();
65 OLED_IIC_Write_Byte(0x78); // Slave address
66 OLED_IIC_Write_Byte(0x40); // Data mode
67 OLED_IIC_Write_Byte(data);
68 OLED_IIC_Stop();
69}
70
71void OLED_SetPos(u8 x, u8 y)
72{
73 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xb0 + y);
74 OLED_Write_Cmd(((x & 0xf0) >> 4) | 0x10);
75 OLED_Write_Cmd((x & 0x0f) | 0x01);
76}
77
78void OLED_Clear(void)
79{
80 u8 i, n;
81 for(i=0; i<8; i++)
82 {
83 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xb0 + i);
84 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x00);
85 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x10);
86 for(n=0; n<128; n++) OLED_Write_Data(0);
87 }
88}
89
90void OLED_ShowChar(u8 x, u8 y, u8 chr, u8 size)
91{
92 u8 c = 0, i = 0;
93 c = chr - ' ';
94 if(x > 128 - 1) { x = 0; y = y + 2; }
95 if(size == 16)
96 {
97 OLED_SetPos(x, y);
98 for(i=0; i<8; i++) OLED_Write_Data(F8X16[c*16+i]);
99 OLED_SetPos(x, y+1);
100 for(i=0; i<8; i++) OLED_Write_Data(F8X16[c*16+i+8]);
101 }
102}
103
104void OLED_ShowString(u8 x, u8 y, u8 *chr, u8 size)
105{
106 u8 j = 0;
107 while(chr[j] != '\0')
108 {
109 OLED_ShowChar(x, y, chr[j], size);
110 x += 8;
111 if(x > 120) { x = 0; y += 2; }
112 j++;
113 }
114}
115
116void OLED_Init(void)
117{
118 GPIO_InitTypeDef GPIO_InitStructure;
119 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOB, ENABLE);
120
121 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin = OLED_SCL_PIN | OLED_SDA_PIN;
122 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_OUT;
123 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_OType = GPIO_OType_OD;
124 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_UP;
125 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Speed = GPIO_Speed_50MHz;
126 GPIO_Init(OLED_IIC_PORT, &GPIO_InitStructure);
127
128 OLED_SCL = 1;
129 OLED_SDA = 1;
130
131 delay_ms(100);
132
133 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xAE); // display off
134 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x20); // Set Memory Addressing Mode
135 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x10); // 00,Horizontal Addressing Mode;01,Vertical Addressing Mode;10,Page Addressing Mode (RESET);11,Invalid
136 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xb0); // Set Page Start Address for Page Addressing Mode,0-7
137 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xc8); // Set COM Output Scan Direction
138 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x00); // set low column address
139 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x10); // set high column address
140 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x40); // set start line address
141 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x81); // set contrast control register
142 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xdf);
143 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xa1); // set segment re-map 0 to 127
144 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xa6); // set normal display
145 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xa8); // set multiplex ratio(1 to 64)
146 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x3F); //
147 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xa4); // 0xa4,Output follows RAM content;0xa5,Output ignores RAM content
148 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xd3); // set display offset
149 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x00); // not offset
150 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xd5); // set display clock divide ratio/oscillator frequency
151 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xf0); // set divide ratio
152 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xd9); // set pre-charge period
153 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x22); //
154 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xda); // set com pins hardware configuration
155 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x12);
156 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xdb); // set vcomh
157 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x20); // 0x20,0.77xVcc
158 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x8d); // set DC-DC enable
159 OLED_Write_Cmd(0x14); //
160 OLED_Write_Cmd(0xaf); // turn on oled panel
161
162 OLED_Clear();
163}

1#include "pwm.h"
2
3/************************************
4引脚连接说明
5LED0连接在PF9,低电平灯亮；高电平，灯灭
6TIM14_CH1(TIM14 -- APB1 16位 84MHZ)
7*************************************/
8void Pwm_PF9_Init(void)
9{
10 TIM_TimeBaseInitTypeDef TIM_TimeBaseStructure;
11 TIM_OCInitTypeDef TIM_OCInitStructure;
12 GPIO_InitTypeDef GPIO_InitStructure;
13
14
15 //使能定时器14
16 RCC_APB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_APB1Periph_TIM14, ENABLE);
17
18 //使能GPIOF组时钟
19 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOF, ENABLE);
20
21
22 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin = GPIO_Pin_9;
23 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_AF; //复用模式
24 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Speed = GPIO_Speed_25MHz;
25 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_OType = GPIO_OType_PP;
26 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_UP ;
27 GPIO_Init(GPIOF, &GPIO_InitStructure);
28
29 //引脚映射 选定引脚与外设关系
30 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOF, GPIO_PinSource9, GPIO_AF_TIM14);
31
32
33
34 /* Time base configuration */
35 TIM_TimeBaseStructure.TIM_Period = (1000-1); //Period(ARR)
36 TIM_TimeBaseStructure.TIM_Prescaler = 83; //84分频 1MHZ
37 TIM_TimeBaseStructure.TIM_ClockDivision = 0;
38 TIM_TimeBaseStructure.TIM_CounterMode = TIM_CounterMode_Up;
39
40 TIM_TimeBaseInit(TIM14, &TIM_TimeBaseStructure);
41
42 /* PWM1 Mode configuration: Channel1 */
43 TIM_OCInitStructure.TIM_OCMode = TIM_OCMode_PWM1; //模式1
44 TIM_OCInitStructure.TIM_OutputState = TIM_OutputState_Enable;
45 TIM_OCInitStructure.TIM_Pulse = 0; //捕获/比较器的初始值
46 TIM_OCInitStructure.TIM_OCPolarity = TIM_OCPolarity_Low;//输出极性，这里设置为低
47 //通道1对应的是OC1
48 TIM_OC1Init(TIM14, &TIM_OCInitStructure);
49
50 //使能预装载寄存器：
51 TIM_OC1PreloadConfig(TIM14, TIM_OCPreload_Enable);
52
53 //使能自动重装载的预装载寄存器允许位
54 TIM_ARRPreloadConfig(TIM14, ENABLE);
55
56 /* TIM3 enable counter */
57 TIM_Cmd(TIM14, ENABLE);
58
59
60}
61
62/************************************
63引脚连接说明
64开锁控制：
65PA8: 继电器控制引脚，默认输出低电平(0)，开锁时输出高电平(1)
66*************************************/
67void Lock_Relay_Init(void)
68{
69 GPIO_InitTypeDef GPIO_InitStructure;
70
71 // 使能 GPIOA 组时钟
72 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOA, ENABLE);
73
74 // 初始化 PA8 为普通推挽输出 (常态低电平)
75 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin = GPIO_Pin_8;
76 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_OUT;
77 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Speed = GPIO_Speed_50MHz;
78 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_OType = GPIO_OType_PP;
79 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_DOWN; // 下拉，确保上电瞬间为低
80 GPIO_Init(GPIOA, &GPIO_InitStructure);
81
82 // 默认初始值为 0 (关锁)
83 GPIO_ResetBits(GPIOA, GPIO_Pin_8);
84}
85
86// 设置继电器状态 (1: 高电平开锁, 0: 低电平关锁)
87void Lock_Set_Relay(uint8_t state)
88{
89 if(state == 1)
90 {
91 GPIO_SetBits(GPIOA, GPIO_Pin_8); // 输出高电平
92 }
93 else
94 {
95 GPIO_ResetBits(GPIOA, GPIO_Pin_8); // 输出低电平
96 }
97}

14// ==================== 门卡存储（FLASH永久保存） ====================
15uint8_t g_enroll_card_mode = 0; // 录入模式
16uint8_t Auto_Card_Flag = 1; // 开机默认启动自动寻卡
17static uint8_t card_list[MAX_CARD_NUM][CARD_LEN]; // 卡号数组
18static uint8_t card_cnt = 0; // 已录入数量

20// SPI底层（不变）
21static uint8_t RC522_SPI_RW(uint8_t byte)
22{
23 uint8_t i, res = 0;
24 for(i=0; i<8; i++)
25 {
26 GPIO_ResetBits(RC522_SCK_PORT, RC522_SCK_PIN);
27 delay_us(5);
28
29 if(byte & 0x80)
30 {
31 GPIO_SetBits(RC522_MOSI_PORT, RC522_MOSI_PIN);
32 }
33 else
34 {
35 GPIO_ResetBits(RC522_MOSI_PORT, RC522_MOSI_PIN);
36 }
37
38 byte <<= 1;
39 delay_us(5);
40 GPIO_SetBits(RC522_SCK_PORT, RC522_SCK_PIN);
41 delay_us(5);
42 res <<= 1;
43 if(GPIO_ReadInputDataBit(RC522_MISO_PORT, RC522_MISO_PIN))
44 {
45 res |= 1;
46 }
47 delay_us(5);
48 }
49 return res;
50}
51
52void RC522_WriteReg(uint8_t addr, uint8_t data)
53{
54 RC522_CS_LOW();
55 RC522_SPI_RW((addr << 1) & 0x7E);
56 RC522_SPI_RW(data);
57 RC522_CS_HIGH();
58}
59
60uint8_t RC522_ReadReg(uint8_t addr)
61{
62 uint8_t data;
63 RC522_CS_LOW();
64 RC522_SPI_RW(((addr << 1) & 0x7E) | 0x80);
65 data = RC522_SPI_RW(0xFF);
66 RC522_CS_HIGH();
67 return data;
68}
69
70static void RC522_SetBit(uint8_t addr, uint8_t mask)
71{
72 RC522_WriteReg(addr, RC522_ReadReg(addr) | mask);
73}
74
75static void RC522_ClearBit(uint8_t addr, uint8_t mask)
76{
77 RC522_WriteReg(addr, RC522_ReadReg(addr) & ~mask);
78}
79
80void RC522_Hard_Reset(void)
81{
82 RC522_RST_LOW();
83 delay_ms(10);
84 RC522_RST_HIGH();
85 delay_ms(10);
86}
87
88void RC522_AntennaOn(void)
89{
90 uint8_t temp=RC522_ReadReg(0x14);
91 if((temp&3)!=3)
92 {
93 RC522_WriteReg(0x14,temp|3);
94 }
95}
96
97void RC522_AntennaOff(void)
98{
99 uint8_t temp=RC522_ReadReg(0x14);
100 RC522_WriteReg(0x14,temp&~3);
101}
102
103// RC522初始化（不变）
104void RC522_Init(void)
105{
106 GPIO_InitTypeDef GPIO_InitStructure;
107 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOB|RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOG, ENABLE);
108
109 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Mode=GPIO_Mode_OUT;
110 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_OType=GPIO_OType_PP;
111 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Speed=GPIO_Speed_50MHz;
112 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_PuPd=GPIO_PuPd_NOPULL;
113 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin=RC522_SCK_PIN|RC522_MOSI_PIN;
114 GPIO_Init(RC522_SCK_PORT,&GPIO_InitStructure);
115
116 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin=RC522_CS_PIN|RC522_RST_PIN;
117 GPIO_Init(RC522_CS_PORT,&GPIO_InitStructure);
118
119 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Mode=GPIO_Mode_IN;
120 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_PuPd=GPIO_PuPd_UP;
121 GPIO_InitStructure.GPIO_Pin=RC522_MISO_PIN;
122 GPIO_Init(RC522_MISO_PORT,&GPIO_InitStructure);
123
124 RC522_CS_HIGH();
125 RC522_RST_HIGH();
126 delay_ms(10);
127
128 RC522_Hard_Reset();
129 RC522_WriteReg(0x01,PCD_RESETPHASE);
130 delay_ms(10);
131
132 RC522_WriteReg(0x2A,0x80);
133 RC522_WriteReg(0x2B,0xA9);
134 RC522_WriteReg(0x2C,0x00);
135 RC522_WriteReg(0x2D,0x30);
136 RC522_WriteReg(0x15,0x40);
137 RC522_WriteReg(0x11,0x3D);
138 RC522_WriteReg(0x14,0x83);
139 RC522_WriteReg(0x26,0x7F);
140 RC522_WriteReg(0x12,0x00);
141 RC522_WriteReg(0x13,0x00);
142 RC522_AntennaOn();
143 delay_ms(10);
144
145 RC522_Flash_LoadCard(); // 开机自动加载FLASH里的卡号
146 printf("已加载%d张门卡\r\n", card_cnt);
147}
148
149// 通信底层（不变）
150static uint8_t RC522_Transceive(uint8_t *sendData,uint8_t sendLen,uint8_t *recvData,uint16_t *recvBits)
151{
152 uint8_t status=1,n;
153 uint32_t timeout=100000;
154
155 RC522_WriteReg(0x02,0x77|0x80);
156 RC522_WriteReg(0x04,0x7F);
157 RC522_SetBit(0x0A,0x80);
158 RC522_WriteReg(0x01,PCD_IDLE);
159
160 for(n=0;n<sendLen;n++)
161 {
162 RC522_WriteReg(0x09,sendData[n]);
163 }
164
165 RC522_WriteReg(0x01,PCD_TRANSCEIVE);
166 RC522_SetBit(0x0D,0x80);
167
168 while(timeout--)
169 {
170 n=RC522_ReadReg(0x04);
171 if(n&0x30)
172 {
173 status=0;
174 break;
175 }
176 if(n&1)
177 {
178 break;
179 }
180 }
181 RC522_ClearBit(0x0D,0x80);
182 if(status==0)
183 {
184 n=RC522_ReadReg(0x06);
185 if(n&0x1B)
186 {
187 status=2;
188 }
189 else
190 {
191 n=RC522_ReadReg(0x0A);
192 uint8_t lb=RC522_ReadReg(0x0C)&7;
193 *recvBits=lb?(n-1)*8+lb:n*8;
194
195 if(n==0)
196 {
197 n=1;
198 }
199 if(n>16)
200 {
201 n=16;
202 }
203
204 for(uint8_t i=0;i<n;i++)
205 {
206 recvData[i]=RC522_ReadReg(0x09);
207 }
208 }
209 }
210 return status;
211}
212
213uint8_t RC522_Request(uint8_t reqCode,uint8_t *cardType)
214{
215 uint8_t status;
216 uint16_t rb;
217 uint8_t sb[2],rbuff[2];
218 RC522_WriteReg(0x0D,0x07);
219 sb[0]=reqCode;
220
221 status=RC522_Transceive(sb,1,rbuff,&rb);
222
223 if(status==0&&rb==16)
224 {
225 cardType[0]=rbuff[0];
226 cardType[1]=rbuff[1];
227 }
228 else
229 {
230 status=1;
231 }
232 RC522_WriteReg(0x0D,0x00);
233 return status;
234}
235
236uint8_t RC522_Anticoll(uint8_t *sn)
237{
238 uint8_t status,i,chk=0;
239 uint16_t rb;
240 uint8_t sb[7],rbuff[7];
241 sb[0]=PICC_ANTICOLL;
242 sb[1]=0x20;
243 status=RC522_Transceive(sb,2,rbuff,&rb);
244
245 if(status||rb!=40)
246 {
247 return 1;
248 }
249
250 for(i=0;i<4;i++)
251 {
252 sn[i]=rbuff[i];
253 chk^=rbuff[i];
254 }
255 return chk!=rbuff[4]?3:0;
256}
257
258// ==================== FLASH读写（掉电保存） ====================
259// 从FLASH加载卡号
260void RC522_Flash_LoadCard(void)
261{
262 uint8_t *p = (uint8_t*)FLASH_SAVE_ADDR;
263 card_cnt = p[0];
264 if(card_cnt > MAX_CARD_NUM)
265 {
266 card_cnt = 0;
267 }
268 for(uint8_t i=0; i<card_cnt; i++)
269 {
270 memcpy(card_list[i], p+1+i*CARD_LEN, CARD_LEN);
271 }
272}
273
274// 保存卡号到FLASH
275void RC522_Flash_SaveCard(void)
276{
277 FLASH_Unlock();
278 FLASH_ClearFlag(FLASH_FLAG_EOP|FLASH_FLAG_OPERR|FLASH_FLAG_WRPERR);
279 FLASH_EraseSector(FLASH_Sector_11, VoltageRange_3); // 擦除扇区
280
281 uint8_t buf[1+MAX_CARD_NUM*CARD_LEN] = {0};
282 buf[0] = card_cnt;
283 for(uint8_t i=0; i<card_cnt; i++)
284 {
285 memcpy(buf+1+i*CARD_LEN, card_list[i], CARD_LEN);
286 }
287
288 for(uint32_t i=0; i<sizeof(buf); i++)
289 {
290 FLASH_ProgramByte(FLASH_SAVE_ADDR+i, buf[i]);
291 }
292 FLASH_Lock();
293}
294
295// 检查卡号是否已存在
296static uint8_t RC522_CheckExist(uint8_t *sn)
297{
298 for(uint8_t i=0; i<card_cnt; i++)
299 {
300 if(memcmp(card_list[i], sn, CARD_LEN)==0)
301 {
302 return 1;
303 }
304 }
305 return 0;
306}
307
308// 录入卡号
309static uint8_t RC522_AddCard(uint8_t *sn)
310{
311 if(card_cnt >= MAX_CARD_NUM)
312 {
313 return 2;
314 }
315 if(RC522_CheckExist(sn))
316 {
317 return 1;
318 }
319 memcpy(card_list[card_cnt], sn, CARD_LEN);
320 card_cnt++;
321 RC522_Flash_SaveCard(); // 写入FLASH永久保存
322 return 0;
323}
324
325// 新增：删除所有门卡
326void RC522_DeleteAllCard(void)
327{
328 card_cnt = 0; // 清空卡计数
329 memset(card_list, 0, sizeof(card_list)); // 清空卡号列表
330 RC522_Flash_SaveCard(); // 同步到FLASH
331 printf("=== 【提示】所有门卡已删除！ ===\r\n");
332}
333
334// ==================== 核心：卡处理逻辑 ====================
335void RC522_Card_Process(void)
336{
337 uint8_t cardSN[4], cardType[2];
338 static uint32_t delay_cnt = 0;
339 if(++delay_cnt < 10)
340 {
341 return; // 10ms轮询，防卡死
342 }
343 delay_cnt = 0;
344
345 // 1. 按键27录入模式
346 if(g_enroll_card_mode)
347 {
348 if(RC522_Request(PICC_REQIDL, cardType)==0 && RC522_Anticoll(cardSN)==0)
349 {
350 printf("录入卡号：%02X%02X%02X%02X\r\n",cardSN[0],cardSN[1],cardSN[2],cardSN[3]);
351 uint8_t res = RC522_AddCard(cardSN);
352 if(res==0)
353 {
354 printf("录入成功！共%d张\r\n",card_cnt);
355 Finger_Led(2);
356 Auto_Card_Flag = 1; // 录入成功后切回自动寻卡模式
357 printf("自动寻卡模式已恢复\r\n");
358 }
359 else if(res==1)
360 {
361 printf("卡号已存在\r\n");
362 Finger_Led(1);
363 }
364 else if(res==2)
365 {
366 printf("卡数量已满\r\n");
367 Finger_Led(1);
368 }
369 g_enroll_card_mode = 0;
370 delay_ms(1000);
371 Finger_Led(4);
372 }
373 }
374 // 2. 自动寻卡验证模式（开机默认启动）
375 else if(Auto_Card_Flag)
376 {
377 if(RC522_Request(PICC_REQIDL, cardType)==0 && RC522_Anticoll(cardSN)==0)
378 {
379 printf("验证卡号：%02X%02X%02X%02X\r\n",cardSN[0],cardSN[1],cardSN[2],cardSN[3]);
380 if(RC522_CheckExist(cardSN))
381 {
382 printf("验证通过，开锁！\r\n");
383 SmartLock_ShowWelcome();
384 Finger_Led(2);
385 Lock_Set_Relay(1);
386 delay_s(3);
387 Lock_Set_Relay(0);
388 SmartLock_ShowBootScreen();
389 }
390 else
391 {
392 printf("未录入，拒绝开锁\r\n");
393 SmartLock_ShowDenied();
394 Finger_Led(1);
395 delay_ms(2000);
396 SmartLock_ShowBootScreen();
397 }
398 Finger_Led(4);
399 delay_ms(1000);
400 }
401 }
402}
