6#if defined(SSD1306_USE_I2C)
7
8void ssd1306_Reset(void) {
9 /* for I2C - do nothing */
10}
11
12// Send a byte to the command register
13void ssd1306_WriteCommand(uint8_t byte) {
14 HAL_I2C_Mem_Write(&SSD1306_I2C_PORT, SSD1306_I2C_ADDR, 0x00, 1, &byte, 1, HAL_MAX_DELAY);
15}
16
17// Send data
18void ssd1306_WriteData(uint8_t* buffer, size_t buff_size) {
19 HAL_I2C_Mem_Write(&SSD1306_I2C_PORT, SSD1306_I2C_ADDR, 0x40, 1, buffer, buff_size, HAL_MAX_DELAY);
20}
21
22#elif defined(SSD1306_USE_SPI)
23
24void ssd1306_Reset(void) {
25 // CS = High (not selected)
26 HAL_GPIO_WritePin(SSD1306_CS_Port, SSD1306_CS_Pin, GPIO_PIN_SET);
27
28 // Reset the OLED
29 HAL_GPIO_WritePin(SSD1306_Reset_Port, SSD1306_Reset_Pin, GPIO_PIN_RESET);
30 HAL_Delay(10);
31 HAL_GPIO_WritePin(SSD1306_Reset_Port, SSD1306_Reset_Pin, GPIO_PIN_SET);
32 HAL_Delay(10);
33}
34
35// Send a byte to the command register
36void ssd1306_WriteCommand(uint8_t byte) {
37 HAL_GPIO_WritePin(SSD1306_CS_Port, SSD1306_CS_Pin, GPIO_PIN_RESET); // select OLED
38 HAL_GPIO_WritePin(SSD1306_DC_Port, SSD1306_DC_Pin, GPIO_PIN_RESET); // command
39 HAL_SPI_Transmit(&SSD1306_SPI_PORT, (uint8_t *) &byte, 1, HAL_MAX_DELAY);
40 HAL_GPIO_WritePin(SSD1306_CS_Port, SSD1306_CS_Pin, GPIO_PIN_SET); // un-select OLED
41}
42
43// Send data
44void ssd1306_WriteData(uint8_t* buffer, size_t buff_size) {
45 HAL_GPIO_WritePin(SSD1306_CS_Port, SSD1306_CS_Pin, GPIO_PIN_RESET); // select OLED
46 HAL_GPIO_WritePin(SSD1306_DC_Port, SSD1306_DC_Pin, GPIO_PIN_SET); // data
47 HAL_SPI_Transmit(&SSD1306_SPI_PORT, buffer, buff_size, HAL_MAX_DELAY);
48 HAL_GPIO_WritePin(SSD1306_CS_Port, SSD1306_CS_Pin, GPIO_PIN_SET); // un-select OLED
49}
50
51#else
52#error "You should define SSD1306_USE_SPI or SSD1306_USE_I2C macro"
53#endif
54
55
56// Screenbuffer
57static uint8_t SSD1306_Buffer[SSD1306_BUFFER_SIZE];
58
59// Screen object
60static SSD1306_t SSD1306;
61
62/* Fills the Screenbuffer with values from a given buffer of a fixed length */
63SSD1306_Error_t ssd1306_FillBuffer(uint8_t* buf, uint32_t len) {
64 SSD1306_Error_t ret = SSD1306_ERR;
65 if (len <= SSD1306_BUFFER_SIZE) {
66 memcpy(SSD1306_Buffer,buf,len);
67 ret = SSD1306_OK;
68 }
69 return ret;
70}
71
72/* Initialize the oled screen */
73void ssd1306_Init(void) {
74 // Reset OLED
75 ssd1306_Reset();
76
77 // Wait for the screen to boot
78 HAL_Delay(100);
79
80 // Init OLED
81 ssd1306_SetDisplayOn(0); //display off
82
83 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x20); //Set Memory Addressing Mode
84 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x00); // 00b,Horizontal Addressing Mode; 01b,Vertical Addressing Mode;
85 // 10b,Page Addressing Mode (RESET); 11b,Invalid
86
87 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xB0); //Set Page Start Address for Page Addressing Mode,0-7
88
89#ifdef SSD1306_MIRROR_VERT
90 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xC0); // Mirror vertically
91#else
92 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xC8); //Set COM Output Scan Direction
93#endif
94
95 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x00); //---set low column address
96 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x10); //---set high column address
97
98 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x40); //--set start line address - CHECK
99
100 ssd1306_SetContrast(0xFF);
101
102#ifdef SSD1306_MIRROR_HORIZ
103 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xA0); // Mirror horizontally
104#else
105 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xA1); //--set segment re-map 0 to 127 - CHECK
106#endif
107
108#ifdef SSD1306_INVERSE_COLOR
109 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xA7); //--set inverse color
110#else
111 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xA6); //--set normal color
112#endif
113
114// Set multiplex ratio.
115#if (SSD1306_HEIGHT == 128)
116 // Found in the Luma Python lib for SH1106.
117 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xFF);
118#else
119 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xA8); //--set multiplex ratio(1 to 64) - CHECK
120#endif
121
122#if (SSD1306_HEIGHT == 32)
123 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x1F); //
124#elif (SSD1306_HEIGHT == 64)
125 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x3F); //
126#elif (SSD1306_HEIGHT == 128)
127 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x3F); // Seems to work for 128px high displays too.
128#else
129#error "Only 32, 64, or 128 lines of height are supported!"
130#endif
131
132 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xA4); //0xa4,Output follows RAM content;0xa5,Output ignores RAM content
133
134 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xD3); //-set display offset - CHECK
135 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x00); //-not offset
136
137 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xD5); //--set display clock divide ratio/oscillator frequency
138 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xF0); //--set divide ratio
139
140 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xD9); //--set pre-charge period
141 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x22); //
142
143 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xDA); //--set com pins hardware configuration - CHECK
144#if (SSD1306_HEIGHT == 32)
145 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x02);
146#elif (SSD1306_HEIGHT == 64)
147 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x12);
148#elif (SSD1306_HEIGHT == 128)
149 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x12);
150#else
151#error "Only 32, 64, or 128 lines of height are supported!"
152#endif
153
154 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xDB); //--set vcomh
155 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x20); //0x20,0.77xVcc
156
157 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x8D); //--set DC-DC enable
158 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x14); //
159 ssd1306_SetDisplayOn(1); //--turn on SSD1306 panel
160
161 // Clear screen
162 ssd1306_Fill(Black);
163
164 // Flush buffer to screen
165 ssd1306_UpdateScreen();
166
167 // Set default values for screen object
168 SSD1306.CurrentX = 0;
169 SSD1306.CurrentY = 0;
170
171 SSD1306.Initialized = 1;
172}
173
174/* Fill the whole screen with the given color */
175void ssd1306_Fill(SSD1306_COLOR color) {
176 memset(SSD1306_Buffer, (color == Black) ? 0x00 : 0xFF, sizeof(SSD1306_Buffer));
177}
178
179/* Write the screenbuffer with changed to the screen */
180void ssd1306_UpdateScreen(void) {
181 // Write data to each page of RAM. Number of pages
182 // depends on the screen height:
183 //
184 // * 32px == 4 pages
185 // * 64px == 8 pages
186 // * 128px == 16 pages
187 for(uint8_t i = 0; i < SSD1306_HEIGHT/8; i++) {
188 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0xB0 + i); // Set the current RAM page address.
189 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x00 + SSD1306_X_OFFSET_LOWER);
190 ssd1306_WriteCommand(0x10 + SSD1306_X_OFFSET_UPPER);
191 ssd1306_WriteData(&SSD1306_Buffer[SSD1306_WIDTH*i],SSD1306_WIDTH);
192 }
193}
194
195/*
196 * Draw one pixel in the screenbuffer
197 * X => X Coordinate
198 * Y => Y Coordinate
199 * color => Pixel color
200 */
201void ssd1306_DrawPixel(uint8_t x, uint8_t y, SSD1306_COLOR color) {
202 if(x >= SSD1306_WIDTH || y >= SSD1306_HEIGHT) {
203 // Don't write outside the buffer
204 return;
205 }
206
207 // Draw in the right color
208 if(color == White) {
209 SSD1306_Buffer[x + (y / 8) * SSD1306_WIDTH] |= 1 << (y % 8);
210 } else {
211 SSD1306_Buffer[x + (y / 8) * SSD1306_WIDTH] &= ~(1 << (y % 8));
212 }
213}
214
215/*
216 * Draw 1 char to the screen buffer
217 * ch => char om weg te schrijven
218 * Font => Font waarmee we gaan schrijven
219 * color => Black or White
220 */
221char ssd1306_WriteChar(char ch, SSD1306_Font_t Font, SSD1306_COLOR color) {
222 uint32_t i, b, j;
223
224 // Check if character is valid
225 if (ch < 32 || ch > 126)
226 return 0;
227
228 // Char width is not equal to font width for proportional font
229 const uint8_t char_width = Font.char_width ? Font.char_width[ch-32] : Font.width;
230 // Check remaining space on current line
231 if (SSD1306_WIDTH < (SSD1306.CurrentX + char_width) ||
232 SSD1306_HEIGHT < (SSD1306.CurrentY + Font.height))
233 {
234 // Not enough space on current line
235 return 0;
236 }
237
238 // Use the font to write
239 for(i = 0; i < Font.height; i++) {
240 b = Font.data[(ch - 32) * Font.height + i];
241 for(j = 0; j < char_width; j++) {
242 if((b << j) & 0x8000) {
243 ssd1306_DrawPixel(SSD1306.CurrentX + j, (SSD1306.CurrentY + i), (SSD1306_COLOR) color);
244 } else {
245 ssd1306_DrawPixel(SSD1306.CurrentX + j, (SSD1306.CurrentY + i), (SSD1306_COLOR)!color);
246 }
247 }
248 }
249
250 // The current space is now taken
251 SSD1306.CurrentX += char_width;
252
253 // Return written char for validation
254 return ch;
255}
256
257/* Write full string to screenbuffer */
258char ssd1306_WriteString(char* str, SSD1306_Font_t Font, SSD1306_COLOR color) {
259 while (*str) {
260 if (ssd1306_WriteChar(*str, Font, color) != *str) {
261 // Char could not be written
262 return *str;
263 }
264 str++;
265 }
266
267 // Everything ok
268 return *str;
269}
270
271/* Position the cursor */
272void ssd1306_SetCursor(uint8_t x, uint8_t y) {
273 SSD1306.CurrentX = x;
274 SSD1306.CurrentY = y;
275}
276
277/* Draw line by Bresenhem's algorithm */
278void ssd1306_Line(uint8_t x1, uint8_t y1, uint8_t x2, uint8_t y2, SSD1306_COLOR color) {
279 int32_t deltaX = abs(x2 - x1);
280 int32_t deltaY = abs(y2 - y1);
281 int32_t signX = ((x1 < x2) ? 1 : -1);
282 int32_t signY = ((y1 < y2) ? 1 : -1);
283 int32_t error = deltaX - deltaY;
284 int32_t error2;
285
286 ssd1306_DrawPixel(x2, y2, color);
287
288 while((x1 != x2) || (y1 != y2)) {
289 ssd1306_DrawPixel(x1, y1, color);
290 error2 = error * 2;
291 if(error2 > -deltaY) {
292 error -= deltaY;
293 x1 += signX;
294 }
295
296 if(error2 < deltaX) {
297 error += deltaX;
298 y1 += signY;
299 }
300 }
301 return;
302}
303
304/* Draw polyline */
305void ssd1306_Polyline(const SSD1306_VERTEX *par_vertex, uint16_t par_size, SSD1306_COLOR color) {
306 uint16_t i;
307 if(par_vertex == NULL) {
308 return;
309 }
310
311 for(i = 1; i < par_size; i++) {
312 ssd1306_Line(par_vertex[i - 1].x, par_vertex[i - 1].y, par_vertex[i].x, par_vertex[i].y, color);
313 }
314
315 return;
316}
317
318/* Convert Degrees to Radians */
319static float ssd1306_DegToRad(float par_deg) {
320 return par_deg * (3.14f / 180.0f);
321}
322
323/* Normalize degree to [0;360] */
324static uint16_t ssd1306_NormalizeTo0_360(uint16_t par_deg) {
325 uint16_t loc_angle;
326 if(par_deg <= 360) {
327 loc_angle = par_deg;
328 } else {
329 loc_angle = par_deg % 360;
330 loc_angle = (loc_angle ? loc_angle : 360);
331 }
332 return loc_angle;
333}
334
335/*
336 * DrawArc. Draw angle is beginning from 4 quart of trigonometric circle (3pi/2)
337 * start_angle in degree
338 * sweep in degree
339 */
340void ssd1306_DrawArc(uint8_t x, uint8_t y, uint8_t radius, uint16_t start_angle, uint16_t sweep, SSD1306_COLOR color) {
341 static const uint8_t CIRCLE_APPROXIMATION_SEGMENTS = 36;
342 float approx_degree;
343 uint32_t approx_segments;
344 uint8_t xp1,xp2;
345 uint8_t yp1,yp2;
346 uint32_t count;
347 uint32_t loc_sweep;
348 float rad;
349
350 loc_sweep = ssd1306_NormalizeTo0_360(sweep);
351
352 count = (ssd1306_NormalizeTo0_360(start_angle) * CIRCLE_APPROXIMATION_SEGMENTS) / 360;
353 approx_segments = (loc_sweep * CIRCLE_APPROXIMATION_SEGMENTS) / 360;
354 approx_degree = loc_sweep / (float)approx_segments;
355 while(count < approx_segments)
356 {
357 rad = ssd1306_DegToRad(count*approx_degree);
358 xp1 = x + (int8_t)(sinf(rad)*radius);
359 yp1 = y + (int8_t)(cosf(rad)*radius);
360 count++;
361 if(count != approx_segments) {
362 rad = ssd1306_DegToRad(count*approx_degree);
363 } else {
364 rad = ssd1306_DegToRad(loc_sweep);
365 }
366 xp2 = x + (int8_t)(sinf(rad)*radius);
367 yp2 = y + (int8_t)(cosf(rad)*radius);
368 ssd1306_Line(xp1,yp1,xp2,yp2,color);
369 }
370
371 return;
372}
373
374/*
375 * Draw arc with radius line
376 * Angle is beginning from 4 quart of trigonometric circle (3pi/2)
377 * start_angle: start angle in degree
378 * sweep: finish angle in degree
379 */
380void ssd1306_DrawArcWithRadiusLine(uint8_t x, uint8_t y, uint8_t radius, uint16_t start_angle, uint16_t sweep, SSD1306_COLOR color) {
381 const uint32_t CIRCLE_APPROXIMATION_SEGMENTS = 36;
382 float approx_degree;
383 uint32_t approx_segments;
384 uint8_t xp1;
385 uint8_t xp2 = 0;
386 uint8_t yp1;
387 uint8_t yp2 = 0;
388 uint32_t count;
389 uint32_t loc_sweep;
390 float rad;
391
392 loc_sweep = ssd1306_NormalizeTo0_360(sweep);
393
394 count = (ssd1306_NormalizeTo0_360(start_angle) * CIRCLE_APPROXIMATION_SEGMENTS) / 360;
395 approx_segments = (loc_sweep * CIRCLE_APPROXIMATION_SEGMENTS) / 360;
396 approx_degree = loc_sweep / (float)approx_segments;
397
398 rad = ssd1306_DegToRad(count*approx_degree);
399 uint8_t first_point_x = x + (int8_t)(sinf(rad)*radius);
400 uint8_t first_point_y = y + (int8_t)(cosf(rad)*radius);
401 while (count < approx_segments) {
402 rad = ssd1306_DegToRad(count*approx_degree);
403 xp1 = x + (int8_t)(sinf(rad)*radius);
404 yp1 = y + (int8_t)(cosf(rad)*radius);
405 count++;
406 if (count != approx_segments) {
407 rad = ssd1306_DegToRad(count*approx_degree);
408 } else {
409 rad = ssd1306_DegToRad(loc_sweep);
410 }
411 xp2 = x + (int8_t)(sinf(rad)*radius);
412 yp2 = y + (int8_t)(cosf(rad)*radius);
413 ssd1306_Line(xp1,yp1,xp2,yp2,color);
414 }
415
416 // Radius line
417 ssd1306_Line(x,y,first_point_x,first_point_y,color);
418 ssd1306_Line(x,y,xp2,yp2,color);
419 return;
420}
421
422/* Draw circle by Bresenhem's algorithm */
423void ssd1306_DrawCircle(uint8_t par_x,uint8_t par_y,uint8_t par_r,SSD1306_COLOR par_color) {
424 int32_t x = -par_r;
425 int32_t y = 0;
426 int32_t err = 2 - 2 * par_r;
427 int32_t e2;
428
429 if (par_x >= SSD1306_WIDTH || par_y >= SSD1306_HEIGHT) {
430 return;
431 }
432
433 do {
434 ssd1306_DrawPixel(par_x - x, par_y + y, par_color);
435 ssd1306_DrawPixel(par_x + x, par_y + y, par_color);
436 ssd1306_DrawPixel(par_x + x, par_y - y, par_color);
437 ssd1306_DrawPixel(par_x - x, par_y - y, par_color);
438 e2 = err;
439
440 if (e2 <= y) {
441 y++;
442 err = err + (y * 2 + 1);
443 if(-x == y && e2 <= x) {
444 e2 = 0;
445 }
446 }
447
448 if (e2 > x) {
449 x++;
450 err = err + (x * 2 + 1);
451 }
452 } while (x <= 0);
453
454 return;
455}
456
457/* Draw filled circle. Pixel positions calculated using Bresenham's algorithm */
458void ssd1306_FillCircle(uint8_t par_x,uint8_t par_y,uint8_t par_r,SSD1306_COLOR par_color) {
459 int32_t x = -par_r;
460 int32_t y = 0;
461 int32_t err = 2 - 2 * par_r;
462 int32_t e2;
463
464 if (par_x >= SSD1306_WIDTH || par_y >= SSD1306_HEIGHT) {
465 return;
466 }
467
468 do {
469 for (uint8_t _y = (par_y + y); _y >= (par_y - y); _y--) {
470 for (uint8_t _x = (par_x - x); _x >= (par_x + x); _x--) {
471 ssd1306_DrawPixel(_x, _y, par_color);
472 }
473 }
474
475 e2 = err;
476 if (e2 <= y) {
477 y++;
478 err = err + (y * 2 + 1);
479 if (-x == y && e2 <= x) {
480 e2 = 0;
481 }
482 }
483
484 if (e2 > x) {
485 x++;
486 err = err + (x * 2 + 1);
487 }
488 } while (x <= 0);
489
490 return;
491}
492
493/* Draw a rectangle */
494void ssd1306_DrawRectangle(uint8_t x1, uint8_t y1, uint8_t x2, uint8_t y2, SSD1306_COLOR color) {
495 ssd1306_Line(x1,y1,x2,y1,color);
496 ssd1306_Line(x2,y1,x2,y2,color);
497 ssd1306_Line(x2,y2,x1,y2,color);
498 ssd1306_Line(x1,y2,x1,y1,color);
499
500 return;
501}
502
503/* Draw a filled rectangle */
504void ssd1306_FillRectangle(uint8_t x1, uint8_t y1, uint8_t x2, uint8_t y2, SSD1306_COLOR color) {
505 uint8_t x_start = ((x1<=x2) ? x1 : x2);
506 uint8_t x_end = ((x1<=x2) ? x2 : x1);
507 uint8_t y_start = ((y1<=y2) ? y1 : y2);
508 uint8_t y_end = ((y1<=y2) ? y2 : y1);
509
510 for (uint8_t y= y_start; (y<= y_end)&&(y<SSD1306_HEIGHT); y++) {
511 for (uint8_t x= x_start; (x<= x_end)&&(x<SSD1306_WIDTH); x++) {
512 ssd1306_DrawPixel(x, y, color);
513 }
514 }
515 return;
516}
517
518SSD1306_Error_t ssd1306_InvertRectangle(uint8_t x1, uint8_t y1, uint8_t x2, uint8_t y2) {
519 if ((x2 >= SSD1306_WIDTH) || (y2 >= SSD1306_HEIGHT)) {
520 return SSD1306_ERR;
521 }
522 if ((x1 > x2) || (y1 > y2)) {
523 return SSD1306_ERR;
524 }
525 uint32_t i;
526 if ((y1 / 8) != (y2 / 8)) {
527 /* if rectangle doesn't lie on one 8px row */
528 for (uint32_t x = x1; x <= x2; x++) {
529 i = x + (y1 / 8) * SSD1306_WIDTH;
530 SSD1306_Buffer[i] ^= 0xFF << (y1 % 8);
531 i += SSD1306_WIDTH;
532 for (; i < x + (y2 / 8) * SSD1306_WIDTH; i += SSD1306_WIDTH) {
533 SSD1306_Buffer[i] ^= 0xFF;
534 }
535 SSD1306_Buffer[i] ^= 0xFF >> (7 - (y2 % 8));
536 }
537 } else {
538 /* if rectangle lies on one 8px row */
539 const uint8_t mask = (0xFF << (y1 % 8)) & (0xFF >> (7 - (y2 % 8)));
540 for (i = x1 + (y1 / 8) * SSD1306_WIDTH;
541 i <= (uint32_t)x2 + (y2 / 8) * SSD1306_WIDTH; i++) {
542 SSD1306_Buffer[i] ^= mask;
543 }
544 }
545 return SSD1306_OK;
546}
547
548/* Draw a bitmap */
549void ssd1306_DrawBitmap(uint8_t x, uint8_t y, const unsigned char* bitmap, uint8_t w, uint8_t h, SSD1306_COLOR color) {
550 int16_t byteWidth = (w + 7) / 8; // Bitmap scanline pad = whole byte
551 uint8_t byte = 0;
552
553 if (x >= SSD1306_WIDTH || y >= SSD1306_HEIGHT) {
554 return;
555 }
556
557 for (uint8_t j = 0; j < h; j++, y++) {
558 for (uint8_t i = 0; i < w; i++) {
559 if (i & 7) {
560 byte <<= 1;
561 } else {
562 byte = (*(const unsigned char *)(&bitmap[j * byteWidth + i / 8]));
563 }
564
565 if (byte & 0x80) {
566 ssd1306_DrawPixel(x + i, y, color);
567 }
568 }
569 }
570 return;
571}
572
573void ssd1306_SetContrast(const uint8_t value) {
574 const uint8_t kSetContrastControlRegister = 0x81;
575 ssd1306_WriteCommand(kSetContrastControlRegister);
576 ssd1306_WriteCommand(value);
577}
578
579void ssd1306_SetDisplayOn(const uint8_t on) {
580 uint8_t value;
581 if (on) {
582 value = 0xAF; // Display on
583 SSD1306.DisplayOn = 1;
584 } else {
585 value = 0xAE; // Display off
586 SSD1306.DisplayOn = 0;
587 }
588 ssd1306_WriteCommand(value);
589}
590
591uint8_t ssd1306_GetDisplayOn() {
592 return SSD1306.DisplayOn;
593}

113// SSD1306 OLED height in pixels
114#ifndef SSD1306_HEIGHT
115#define SSD1306_HEIGHT 64
116#endif
117
118// SSD1306 width in pixels
119#ifndef SSD1306_WIDTH
120#define SSD1306_WIDTH 128
121#endif
122
123#ifndef SSD1306_BUFFER_SIZE
124#define SSD1306_BUFFER_SIZE SSD1306_WIDTH * SSD1306_HEIGHT / 8
125#endif

127// Enumeration for screen colors
128typedef enum {
129 Black = 0x00, // Black color, no pixel
130 White = 0x01 // Pixel is set. Color depends on OLED
131} SSD1306_COLOR;
132
133typedef enum {
134 SSD1306_OK = 0x00,
135 SSD1306_ERR = 0x01 // Generic error.
136} SSD1306_Error_t;
137
138// Struct to store transformations
139typedef struct {
140 uint16_t CurrentX;
141 uint16_t CurrentY;
142 uint8_t Initialized;
143 uint8_t DisplayOn;
144} SSD1306_t;
145
146typedef struct {
147 uint8_t x;
148 uint8_t y;
149} SSD1306_VERTEX;
150
151/** Font */
152typedef struct {
153 const uint8_t width; /**< Font width in pixels */
154 const uint8_t height; /**< Font height in pixels */
155 const uint16_t *const data; /**< Pointer to font data array */
156 const uint8_t *const char_width; /**< Proportional character width in pixels (NULL for monospaced) */
157} SSD1306_Font_t;
158

170void ssd1306_DrawCircle(uint8_t par_x, uint8_t par_y, uint8_t par_r, SSD1306_COLOR color);
171void ssd1306_FillCircle(uint8_t par_x,uint8_t par_y,uint8_t par_r,SSD1306_COLOR par_color);

4//THUMB指令不支持汇编内联
5//采用如下方法实现执行汇编指令WFI
6__asm void WFI_SET(void)
7{
8 WFI;
9}
10//关闭所有中断(但是不包括fault和NMI中断)
11__asm void INTX_DISABLE(void)
12{
13 CPSID I
14 BX LR
15}
16//开启所有中断
17__asm void INTX_ENABLE(void)
18{
19 CPSIE I
20 BX LR
21}
22//设置栈顶地址
23//addr:栈顶地址
24__asm void MSR_MSP(u32 addr)
25{
26 MSR MSP, r0 //set Main Stack value
27 BX r14
28}

7//位带操作,实现51类似的GPIO控制功能
8//具体实现思想,参考<<CM3权威指南>>第五章(87页~92页).M4同M3类似,只是寄存器地址变了.
9//IO口操作宏定义
10#define BITBAND(addr, bitnum) ((addr & 0xF0000000)+0x2000000+((addr &0xFFFFF)<<5)+(bitnum<<2))
11#define MEM_ADDR(addr) *((volatile unsigned long *)(addr))
12#define BIT_ADDR(addr, bitnum) MEM_ADDR(BITBAND(addr, bitnum))
13//IO口地址映射
14#define GPIOA_ODR_Addr (GPIOA_BASE+20) //0x40020014
15#define GPIOB_ODR_Addr (GPIOB_BASE+20) //0x40020414
16#define GPIOC_ODR_Addr (GPIOC_BASE+20) //0x40020814
17#define GPIOD_ODR_Addr (GPIOD_BASE+20) //0x40020C14
18#define GPIOE_ODR_Addr (GPIOE_BASE+20) //0x40021014
19#define GPIOF_ODR_Addr (GPIOF_BASE+20) //0x40021414
20#define GPIOG_ODR_Addr (GPIOG_BASE+20) //0x40021814
21#define GPIOH_ODR_Addr (GPIOH_BASE+20) //0x40021C14
22#define GPIOI_ODR_Addr (GPIOI_BASE+20) //0x40022014
23
24#define GPIOA_IDR_Addr (GPIOA_BASE+16) //0x40020010
25#define GPIOB_IDR_Addr (GPIOB_BASE+16) //0x40020410
26#define GPIOC_IDR_Addr (GPIOC_BASE+16) //0x40020810
27#define GPIOD_IDR_Addr (GPIOD_BASE+16) //0x40020C10
28#define GPIOE_IDR_Addr (GPIOE_BASE+16) //0x40021010
29#define GPIOF_IDR_Addr (GPIOF_BASE+16) //0x40021410
30#define GPIOG_IDR_Addr (GPIOG_BASE+16) //0x40021810
31#define GPIOH_IDR_Addr (GPIOH_BASE+16) //0x40021C10
32#define GPIOI_IDR_Addr (GPIOI_BASE+16) //0x40022010
33
34//IO口操作,只对单一的IO口!
35//确保n的值小于16!
36#define PAout(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOA_ODR_Addr,n) //输出
37#define PAin(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOA_IDR_Addr,n) //输入
38
39#define PBout(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOB_ODR_Addr,n) //输出
40#define PBin(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOB_IDR_Addr,n) //输入
41
42#define PCout(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOC_ODR_Addr,n) //输出
43#define PCin(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOC_IDR_Addr,n) //输入
44
45#define PDout(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOD_ODR_Addr,n) //输出
46#define PDin(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOD_IDR_Addr,n) //输入
47
48#define PEout(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOE_ODR_Addr,n) //输出
49#define PEin(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOE_IDR_Addr,n) //输入
50
51#define PFout(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOF_ODR_Addr,n) //输出
52#define PFin(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOF_IDR_Addr,n) //输入
53
54#define PGout(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOG_ODR_Addr,n) //输出
55#define PGin(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOG_IDR_Addr,n) //输入
56
57#define PHout(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOH_ODR_Addr,n) //输出
58#define PHin(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOH_IDR_Addr,n) //输入
59
60#define PIout(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOI_ODR_Addr,n) //输出
61#define PIin(n) BIT_ADDR(GPIOI_IDR_Addr,n) //输入
62
63//以下为汇编函数
64void WFI_SET(void); //执行WFI指令
65void INTX_DISABLE(void);//关闭所有中断
66void INTX_ENABLE(void); //开启所有中断
67void MSR_MSP(u32 addr); //设置堆栈地址
68#endif

5/*********************************
6定时器说明
7
8TIM3--APB1
9频率：84MHZ
1016位定时器
11
12*********************************/
13void Tim3_Init(void)
14{
15 NVIC_InitTypeDef NVIC_InitStructure;
16 TIM_TimeBaseInitTypeDef TIM_TimeStructure;
17
18 /* TIM3 clock enable */
19 //使能定时器3
20 RCC_APB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_APB1Periph_TIM3, ENABLE);
21
22
23
24
25 /* Time base configuration */
26 TIM_TimeStructure.TIM_Prescaler = (84-1); //84分频 84MHZ/84 = 1MHZ
27 TIM_TimeStructure.TIM_Period = (1000-1); //重载值为1000，在1MHZ，计1000个数，用时1ms
28 TIM_TimeStructure.TIM_CounterMode = TIM_CounterMode_Up; //向上计数
29 TIM_TimeStructure.TIM_ClockDivision = 0; //分频因子
30 TIM_TimeBaseInit(TIM3, &TIM_TimeStructure);
31
32
33 /* Enable the TIM3 gloabal Interrupt */
34 //配置定时器NVIC
35 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannel = TIM3_IRQn;
36 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelPreemptionPriority = 0;
37 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelSubPriority = 1;
38 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelCmd = ENABLE;
39 NVIC_Init(&NVIC_InitStructure);
40
41
42 /* TIM Interrupts enable */
43 //配置为更新中断
44 TIM_ITConfig(TIM3, TIM_IT_Update, ENABLE);
45
46 /* TIM3 enable counter */
47 //使能定时器 开启定时器
48 TIM_Cmd(TIM3, ENABLE);
49
50}

11volatile uint8_t g_usart6_rx_buf[512]={0};

13volatile uint32_t g_usart6_rx_end=0;

16/*********************************
17PA9 ---- USART1_TX(发送端)
18PA10 ---- USART1_RX(接收端)
19*********************************/
20void Usart1_Init(int BaudRate)
21{
22 GPIO_InitTypeDef GPIO_InitStruct;
23 USART_InitTypeDef USART_InitStruct;
24 NVIC_InitTypeDef NVIC_InitStructure;
25
26 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOA, ENABLE);
27 RCC_APB2PeriphClockCmd(RCC_APB2Periph_USART1, ENABLE);
28
29 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Pin = GPIO_Pin_9|GPIO_Pin_10;
30 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_AF;
31 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Speed = GPIO_Speed_25MHz;
32 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_OType = GPIO_OType_PP;
33 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_UP ;
34 GPIO_Init(GPIOA, &GPIO_InitStruct);
35
36 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOA, GPIO_PinSource9, GPIO_AF_USART1);
37 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOA, GPIO_PinSource10, GPIO_AF_USART1);
38
39 USART_InitStruct.USART_BaudRate = BaudRate;
40 USART_InitStruct.USART_Mode = USART_Mode_Tx|USART_Mode_Rx;
41 USART_InitStruct.USART_Parity = USART_Parity_No;
42 USART_InitStruct.USART_StopBits = USART_StopBits_1;
43 USART_InitStruct.USART_WordLength = USART_WordLength_8b;
44 USART_InitStruct.USART_HardwareFlowControl = USART_HardwareFlowControl_None;
45 USART_Init(USART1, &USART_InitStruct);
46
47 // 串口优先级最高，保证接收不丢包
48 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannel = USART1_IRQn;
49 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelPreemptionPriority = 0x00;
50 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelSubPriority = 0x00;
51 NVIC_InitStructure.NVIC_IRQChannelCmd = ENABLE;
52 NVIC_Init(&NVIC_InitStructure);
53
54 USART_ITConfig(USART1, USART_IT_RXNE, ENABLE);
55 USART_Cmd(USART1, ENABLE);
56}
57
58// USART6 初始化 给 FM225 人脸识别用
59// PC6 = TX
60// PC7 = RX
61void usart6_init(uint32_t baudrate)
62{
63 GPIO_InitTypeDef GPIO_InitStruct;
64 USART_InitTypeDef USART_InitStruct;
65 NVIC_InitTypeDef NVIC_InitStruct;
66
67 // 开时钟
68 RCC_AHB1PeriphClockCmd(RCC_AHB1Periph_GPIOC, ENABLE);
69 RCC_APB2PeriphClockCmd(RCC_APB2Periph_USART6, ENABLE);
70
71 // 复用引脚
72 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOC, GPIO_PinSource6, GPIO_AF_USART6);
73 GPIO_PinAFConfig(GPIOC, GPIO_PinSource7, GPIO_AF_USART6);
74
75 // GPIO 配置
76 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Pin = GPIO_Pin_6 | GPIO_Pin_7;
77 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Mode = GPIO_Mode_AF;
78 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_OType = GPIO_OType_PP;
79 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_PuPd = GPIO_PuPd_UP;
80 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Speed = GPIO_Speed_50MHz;
81 GPIO_Init(GPIOC, &GPIO_InitStruct);
82
83 // 串口参数
84 USART_InitStruct.USART_BaudRate = baudrate;
85 USART_InitStruct.USART_WordLength = USART_WordLength_8b;
86 USART_InitStruct.USART_StopBits = USART_StopBits_1;
87 USART_InitStruct.USART_Parity = USART_Parity_No;
88 USART_InitStruct.USART_Mode = USART_Mode_Tx | USART_Mode_Rx;
89 USART_InitStruct.USART_HardwareFlowControl = USART_HardwareFlowControl_None;
90 USART_Init(USART6, &USART_InitStruct);
91
92 // 中断
93 NVIC_InitStruct.NVIC_IRQChannel = USART6_IRQn;
94 NVIC_InitStruct.NVIC_IRQChannelPreemptionPriority = 0;
95 NVIC_InitStruct.NVIC_IRQChannelSubPriority = 1;
96 NVIC_InitStruct.NVIC_IRQChannelCmd = ENABLE;
97 NVIC_Init(&NVIC_InitStruct);
98
99 USART_ITConfig(USART6, USART_IT_RXNE, ENABLE);
100 USART_Cmd(USART6, ENABLE);
101}

103
104void usart_send_str(USART_TypeDef* USARTx,char *str)
105{
106 char *p = str;
107
108 while(*p!='\0')
109 {
110 USART_SendData(USARTx,*p);
111
112 p++;
113
114 //等待数据发送成功
115 while(USART_GetFlagStatus(USARTx,USART_FLAG_TXE)==RESET);
116 USART_ClearFlag(USARTx,USART_FLAG_TXE);
117 }
118}
119
120
121void usart_send_bytes(USART_TypeDef* USARTx,uint8_t *buf,uint32_t len)
122{
123 uint8_t *p = buf;
124
125 while(len--)
126 {
127 USART_SendData(USARTx,*p);
128
129 p++;
130
131 //等待数据发送成功
132 while(USART_GetFlagStatus(USARTx,USART_FLAG_TXE)==RESET);
133 USART_ClearFlag(USARTx,USART_FLAG_TXE);
134 }
135}

140// 缓冲区锁声明，要和 fm225.c 里的定义保持一致
141extern volatile uint8_t g_rx_lock;
142
143void USART6_IRQHandler(void)
144{
145 uint8_t ch;
146 if(USART_GetITStatus(USART6, USART_IT_RXNE) != RESET)
147 {
148 ch = USART_ReceiveData(USART6);
149
150 // 缓冲区锁+溢出保护
151 if(g_rx_lock == 0 && g_usart6_rx_cnt < sizeof(g_usart6_rx_buf))
152 {
153 g_usart6_rx_buf[g_usart6_rx_cnt++] = ch;
154 }
155
156 // 重启超时定时器
157 TIM_Cmd(TIM3, DISABLE);
158 TIM_SetCounter(TIM3, 0);
159 TIM_Cmd(TIM3, ENABLE);
160
161 USART_ClearITPendingBit(USART6, USART_IT_RXNE);
162 }
163}
164
165
166// 在 usart.c 中优化中断，确保即使发生溢出也能快速恢复
167void USART1_IRQHandler(void)
168{
169 uint8_t data;
170 // 1. 强力处理所有异常标志（溢出、噪声、帧错误等）
171 if(USART_GetFlagStatus(USART1, USART_FLAG_ORE) != RESET ||
172 USART_GetFlagStatus(USART1, USART_FLAG_FE) != RESET ||
173 USART_GetFlagStatus(USART1, USART_FLAG_NE) != RESET)
174 {
175 data = USART_ReceiveData(USART1); // 必须读DR才能清除这些标志
176 g_cout = 0; // 发生错误时清空计数，重新寻找帧头
177 return;
178 }
179
180 if(USART_GetITStatus(USART1, USART_IT_RXNE) != RESET)
181 {
182 data = USART_ReceiveData(USART1);
183
184 if(g_cout == 0)
185 {
186 if(data == 0xF5) g_buffer[g_cout++] = data;
187 }
188 else
189 {
190 g_buffer[g_cout++] = data;
191 if(g_cout >= 8)
192 {
193 if(g_buffer[0] == 0xF5 && g_buffer[7] == 0xF5)
194 {
195 memcpy((uint8_t*)g_rx_buffer, (uint8_t*)g_buffer, 8);
196 g_flag = 1;
197 }
198 g_cout = 0;
199 }
200 }
201 USART_ClearITPendingBit(USART1, USART_IT_RXNE);
202 }
203}

20// 指纹相关宏定义（与main.c保持一致）
21#define ACK_SUCCESS 0x00
22#define ACK_FAIL 0x01
23#define ACK_FULL 0x04
24#define ACK_NOUSER 0x05
25#define ACK_USER_EXIST 0x07
26#define ACK_TIMEOUT 0x08

29void zhi_init(void)

33 GPIO_InitStruct.GPIO_Pin = GPIO_Pin_15;

38
39uint8_t Finger_CalChk(uint8_t *data)
40{
41 uint8_t chk = 0;
42 for(uint8_t i=0; i<5; i++) chk ^= data[i];
43 return chk;
44}
45
46void Finger_SendCmd(uint8_t type, uint8_t p1, uint8_t p2, uint8_t p3)
47{
48 uint8_t cmd[8] = {0xF5, type, p1, p2, p3, 0x00, 0, 0xF5};
49 cmd[6] = Finger_CalChk(&cmd[1]);
50
51 __disable_irq();
52 g_flag = 0;
53 g_cout = 0;
54 memset((uint8_t*)g_buffer, 0, 8);
55 memset((uint8_t*)g_rx_buffer, 0, 8);
56 __enable_irq();
57
58 for(uint8_t i=0; i<8; i++)
59 {
60 while(USART_GetFlagStatus(USART1, USART_FLAG_TXE) == RESET);
61 USART_SendData(USART1, cmd[i]);
62 }
63 while(USART_GetFlagStatus(USART1, USART_FLAG_TC) == RESET);
64 delay_ms(20);
65}
66
67void Finger_Led(uint8_t mode)
68{
69 if(mode == 1) Finger_SendCmd(0xC3, 0x03, 0x07, 0x96); // 红灯闪烁
70 else if(mode == 2) Finger_SendCmd(0xC3, 0x05, 0x05, 0x96); // 绿灯常亮
71 else if(mode == 3) Finger_SendCmd(0xC3, 0x06, 0x07, 0x96); // 蓝灯闪烁
72 else if(mode == 4) Finger_SendCmd(0xC3, 0x07, 0x07, 0x96); // 全灭
73}
74
75void Finger_Verify_1N(void)
76{
77 Finger_SendCmd(0x0C, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00);
78}
79
80// 新增：指纹录入处理函数（抽离自main.c）
81void Finger_Enroll_Process(void)
82{
83 if(g_enroll_flag == 1)
84 {
85 g_enroll_flag = 0;
86 delay_ms(15);
87 if(PAin(0) == 0)
88 {
89 while(PAin(0) == 0);
90 if(g_enroll_step == 0 && g_unlock_mode == 1) // 修改：解锁模式默认是1
91 {
92 g_enroll_step = 1;
93 printf("=== 录入第一步：请按手指 ===\r\n");
94 Finger_Led(1);
95 Finger_SendCmd(0x01, (user_id>>8)&0xFF, user_id&0xFF, 0x01);
96 }
97 }
98 }
99
100 // 录入第一步
101 if(g_enroll_step == 1)
102 {
103 uint32_t timeout = 0;
104 while(g_flag == 0 && timeout < 8000) { delay_ms(1); timeout++; }
105
106 if(g_flag == 1)
107 {
108 g_flag = 0;
109 if(g_rx_buffer[1] == 0x01)
110 {
111 if(g_rx_buffer[4] == ACK_SUCCESS)
112 {
113 printf("第一步成功！请抬手指，1秒后按第二次\r\n");
114 Finger_Led(2); delay_ms(1000); Finger_Led(4);
115 g_enroll_step = 2;
116 printf("=== 录入第二步：请按手指 ===\r\n");
117 Finger_Led(1);
118 Finger_SendCmd(0x02, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00);
119 }
120 else if(g_rx_buffer[4] == ACK_USER_EXIST)
121 {
122 printf("=== 该ID已录入！请换一个ID ===\r\n");
123 user_id++;
124 Finger_Led(3); delay_ms(1000); Finger_Led(4);
125 g_enroll_step = 0; // 录入结束，恢复解锁
126 }
127 else
128 {
129 printf("第一步失败！错误码：%02X\r\n", g_rx_buffer[4]);
130 Finger_Led(3); delay_ms(1000); Finger_Led(4);
131 g_enroll_step = 0; // 录入结束，恢复解锁
132 }
133 }
134 }
135 else
136 {
137 printf("第一步超时！\r\n");
138 Finger_Led(3); delay_ms(1000); Finger_Led(4);
139 g_enroll_step = 0; // 录入结束，恢复解锁
140 }
141 }
142
143 // 录入第二步
144 if(g_enroll_step == 2)
145 {
146 uint32_t timeout = 0;
147 while(g_flag == 0 && timeout < 8000) { delay_ms(1); timeout++; }
148
149 if(g_flag == 1)
150 {
151 g_flag = 0;
152 if(g_rx_buffer[1] == 0x02 && g_rx_buffer[4] == ACK_SUCCESS)
153 {
154 printf("第二步成功！请抬手指，1秒后按第三次\r\n");
155 Finger_Led(2); delay_ms(1000); Finger_Led(4);
156 g_enroll_step = 3;
157 printf("=== 录入第三步：请按手指 ===\r\n");
158 Finger_Led(1);
159 Finger_SendCmd(0x03, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00);
160 }
161 else
162 {
163 printf("第二步失败！错误码：%02X\r\n", g_rx_buffer[4]);
164 Finger_Led(3); delay_ms(1000); Finger_Led(4);
165 g_enroll_step = 0; // 录入结束，恢复解锁
166 }
167 }
168 else
169 {
170 printf("第二步超时！\r\n");
171 Finger_Led(3); delay_ms(1000); Finger_Led(4);
172 g_enroll_step = 0; // 录入结束，恢复解锁
173 }
174 }
175
176 // 录入第三步
177 if(g_enroll_step == 3)
178 {
179 uint32_t timeout = 0;
180 while(g_flag == 0 && timeout < 8000)
181 {
182 delay_ms(1);
183 timeout++;
184 if(timeout % 1000 == 0) printf("等待模块应答...%d秒\r\n", timeout/1000);
185 }
186
187 if(g_flag == 1)
188 {
189 g_flag = 0;
190 if(g_rx_buffer[1] == 0x03 && g_rx_buffer[4] == ACK_SUCCESS)
191 {
192 uint16_t final_id = (g_rx_buffer[2] << 8) | g_rx_buffer[3];
193 printf("=== 录入成功！最终用户ID：%d ===\r\n", final_id);
194 user_id++;
195 Finger_Led(2); delay_ms(3000); Finger_Led(4);
196 }
197 else
198 {
199 printf("第三步失败！错误码：%02X\r\n", g_rx_buffer[4]);
200 Finger_Led(3); delay_ms(1000); Finger_Led(4);
201 }
202 }
203 else
204 {
205 printf("第三步超时！模块未应答\r\n");
206 Finger_Led(3); delay_ms(1000); Finger_Led(4);
207 }
208 g_enroll_step = 0; // 录入结束，恢复解锁
209 }
210}
211
212// 移除解锁模式触发逻辑（解锁默认一直开启）
213void Finger_Unlock_Trigger_Process(void)
214{
215 // 清空原有触发逻辑，解锁模式默认开启
216}
217
218// 新增：开锁模式核心逻辑（抽离自main.c）
219void Finger_Unlock_Mode_Process(void)
220{
221 // 指纹录入阶段，关闭解锁功能
222 if(g_enroll_step != 0)
223 {
224 return;
225 }
226
227 // 解锁模式始终开启（g_unlock_mode默认=1）
228 if(g_unlock_mode == 1)
229 {
230 // 检测PG15触摸触发比对
231 if(PGin(15) == 1)
232 {
233 //printf("检测到手指，开始比对...\r\n");
234 Finger_Verify_1N();
235
236 uint32_t timeout = 0;
237 //while(g_flag == 0 && timeout < 8000) { delay_ms(1); timeout++; }
238
239 if(g_flag == 1)
240 {
241 g_flag = 0;
242 if(g_rx_buffer[1] == 0x0C)
243 {
244 uint16_t verify_id = (g_rx_buffer[2] << 8) | g_rx_buffer[3];
245 uint8_t verify_role = g_rx_buffer[4];
246
247 if(verify_id != 0)
248 {
249 printf("=== 开锁成功！用户ID：%d，权限：%d ===\r\n", verify_id, verify_role);
250 Finger_SendCmd(0xC3, 0x05, 0x05, 0x96); // 绿灯常亮
251 SmartLock_ShowScanning();
252 SmartLock_ShowWelcome();
253 Lock_Set_Relay(1);
254 delay_s(3);
255 Lock_Set_Relay(0);
256 SmartLock_ShowBootScreen();
257
258 Finger_SendCmd(0xC3, 0x06, 0x07, 0x96); // 恢复蓝灯闪烁
259 // 不再退出解锁模式，保持开启
260 printf("=== 指纹解锁成功，继续等待指纹验证 ===\r\n");
261 Finger_Led(3); // 蓝灯闪烁，提示继续等待
262 }
263 else
264 {
265 printf("=== 开锁失败：未找到匹配指纹 ===\r\n");
266 Finger_SendCmd(0xC3, 0x03, 0x07, 0x96); // 红灯闪烁
267 delay_ms(1000);
268 Finger_SendCmd(0xC3, 0x06, 0x07, 0x96); // 恢复蓝灯闪烁
269 }
270 }
271 }
272// else
273// {
274// printf("=== 开锁超时：未检测到指纹 ===\r\n");
275// }
276
277 while(PGin(15) == 1); // 等待手指抬开
278 delay_ms(100);
279 }
280
281 // 移除PE2退出解锁模式的逻辑，解锁功能一直开启
282 }
283}
284
285// 新增：删除所有指纹处理（抽离自main.c）
286void Finger_DeleteAll_Process(void)
287{
288 if(g_delete_all_flag == 1)
289 {
290 g_delete_all_flag = 0;
291 delay_ms(15);
292 if(PEin(3) == 0)
293 {
294 while(PEin(3) == 0);
295 if(g_enroll_step == 0 && g_unlock_mode == 1) // 修改：解锁模式默认是1
296 {
297 printf("=== 开始删除所有指纹 ===\r\n");
298 Finger_SendCmd(0xC3, 0x02, 0x07, 0x96); // 红蓝闪烁
299
300 Finger_SendCmd(0x05, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00); // 删除所有指令
301
302 uint32_t timeout = 0;
303 while(g_flag == 0 && timeout < 2000)
304 {
305 delay_ms(1);
306 timeout++;
307 }
308
309 if(g_flag == 1)
310 {
311 g_flag = 0;
312 if(g_rx_buffer[1] == 0x05 && g_rx_buffer[4] == 0x00)
313 {
314 printf("=== 所有指纹删除成功！===\r\n");
315 user_id = 1;
316 Finger_SendCmd(0xC3, 0x05, 0x05, 0x96); // 绿灯常亮
317 delay_ms(2000);
318 }
319 else
320 {
321 printf("=== 删除失败！错误码：%02X ===\r\n", g_rx_buffer[4]);
322 Finger_SendCmd(0xC3, 0x03, 0x07, 0x96); // 红灯闪烁
323 delay_ms(1000);
324 }
325 }
326 else
327 {
328 printf("=== 删除超时！模块无应答 ===\r\n");
329 Finger_SendCmd(0xC3, 0x03, 0x07, 0x96);
330 delay_ms(1000);
331 }
332 Finger_Led(4);
333 }
334 }
335 }
336}
